kathaṃ me vṛttivicchedo bhavadbhyāṃ krīḍayā kṛtaḥ
viṣṇorbhṛtyo 'hamityeṣā nūnamasti vimānanā
varado'haṃ gato yasya vāhanaṃ svecchayākalaḥ
mayāpi nihatā daityā jāto 'hamapi kaśyapāt
athāha nyūnatāṃ kena yuṣmadabhyarthako gataḥ
vahāmi pakṣaprāntena trailokyaṃ viṣṇunā saha
iti vādinam uddarpaṃ taṃ hasanviṣṇurabhyadhāt
savyetaraṃ vaha sakhe bāhuṃ me balināṃ vara
satyamitāṃ tataste 'haṃ jāne vāṇīṃ dhṛtiṃ tathā
ityuktvāsya bhujaṃ skandhe nidadhe sa hi līlayā
adarpaśikṣāguruṇā guruṇā tena so 'patat
vadanodgīrṇarudhiraḥ suptapakṣo 'timūrtitaḥ
saṃrakṣito bhagavatā dayārdreṇa dhṛtiṃ yayau
iti darpo 'vamānāya vināśāyaiva durnayaḥ
duryodhana vṛthā darpaṃ mā kṛthā vyasanodayam
yaśaḥsitajaṭābhārāḥ pṛṣaṅkanakhadanturāḥ
nṛsiṃhā hi mahārāja nṛpabhīmadhanaṃjayāḥ
śrutveti kaṇvavacanaṃ niḥśvasanvalitānanaḥ
spṛśankarikarākāram ūrum ūrīkṛtānayaḥ
gūḍhābhipātairviṣamaṃ lakṣmīsopānavibhramaiḥ
vakṣo vilokya rādheyaṃ tiryaksaṃbhāvayandṛśā
kṛtakasmerakiraṇaiḥ kurvan aparacāmare
pādenovāca vilikhanpādapīṭhaṃ suyodhanaḥ
yāce vadāmi viharāmi harāmi śatrūnpremṇā bhaje nanu parāniti mūḍhavāñchā
daivaṃ hi janmalikhitālikapaṭṭalekhāṃ dṛṣṭvā muhurmuhurudeti śubhāśubheṣu
ityukte dhārtarāṣṭreṇa viṣaṇṇo nārado 'vadat
api kelikalālokaḥ kalahaikakutūhalī
nirbandhāddurgrahāndhānāṃ duḥkhātaṅkaviṣadrumāḥ
svayamuptaiḥ prajāyante hṛdi bījairivānayaiḥ
gālavākhyo muniḥ śiṣyo viśvāmitraṃ guruṃ purā
dadāmi dakṣiṇāṃ tubhyamityavocatpunaḥ punaḥ
pratyākhyāto 'pi bahuśastadeva sa yadāvadat
tato nirbandhakupito viśvāmitrastamabravīt
dakṣiṇāvartaśuddhānāṃ śatānyaṣṭau prayaccha me
hayānāṃ śyāmakarṇānāṃ himakundenduvarcasām
tacchrutvā durlabhānmatvā gālavastadvidhānhayān
dinairevāsthiśeṣo 'bhūccintāśokaparāyaṇaḥ
sa vayasyaṃ samabhyetya garuḍaṃ patatāṃ varam
tamartham anuvedyāsmai śuśocānuśayākulaḥ
tatastamabravīttārkṣyo māmāruhya mune diśaḥ
vicitya śyāmakarṇāṃstān aśvān gurvarthamāpnuhi
ityuktaḥ pakṣirājena tamevāruhya gālavaḥ
udvegamūrchitaḥ prāyādardhamīlitalocanaḥ
sa paśyanvividhāścaryānnāgāngaganasaṅginaḥ
pūrvaṃ pūrvā diśaḥ prāpa devānāṃ pūrvamālayam
purā yamena gurave dakṣiṇāyai niveditām
dakṣiṇāṃ ca tataḥ prāyātpitaro yatra somapāḥ
paścimāṃ ca tato gatvā paścādyatra raviḥ karān
visṛjya vāsarasyānte praviśatyambhasāṃ nidhim
uttarāṃ diśamāsthāya pāpāduttīryate yayā
yasyā viṣṇupadaṃ puṇyaṃ maruttaṃ makhabhūstathā
bhrāntvā diśastā ṛṣabhaḥ prāṃśuṃ bhūdharamāptavān
tasyopaviṣṭau śikhare cirādgaruḍagālavau
tataḥ siddhāṃ dadṛśatuḥ śāṇḍilīṃ nāma bhāsurām
kṛtātithyau tayā tatra bhuktvā nidrāmavāpatuḥ
garuḍo vītanidro 'tha manorathamacintayat
evaṃvidhā munivadhūryogyā brahmaniketane
viṣṇoḥ śakrasya vā dhāmni dhyātveti virarāma saḥ
tataḥ prabhāte visrastapakṣaḥ śīrṇakarānanaḥ
praklinnamāṃsakūṭābho babhūva bhṛśavihvalaḥ
niveditānvayaṃ paścātpraṇataṃ karuṇākulā
sapakṣaṃ śāṇḍilī cakre taṃ dṛśā balavattaram
tāmāmantrya tato yātastārkṣyeṇa saha gālavaḥ
gurvarthacintāvidhuro na dhṛtiṃ pratyapadyata
taṃ vrajantaṃ pathi munirviśvāmitro yadṛcchayā
āyātaḥ sasmito 'vādīnnūnaṃ lajjānatānanam
kva te mahyaṃ pratijñātāḥ śyāmakarṇā hayāstvayā
ityuktvā kauśike yāte gālavaṃ bhṛśaduḥkhitam
uvāca garuḍo dhyātvā tasya kāryasya niścayam
dhanena labhyate sarvaṃ tacca śakradhanādhipau
divyaṃ premṇā mudā yuktau rakṣataḥ pṛthusaṃcayau
prāpyante draviṇenaiva śyāmakarṇāsturaṅgamāḥ
eka eveśvaro rājā yayātiramitānugaḥ
ityuktvā garuḍo gatvā yayātiṃ muninā saha
yajñavyayīkṛtāśeṣadhanamaśvānayācata
so 'bravīdarthitastena śulkadeyāsti me sutā
mādhavī nāma tāmeva vitīryāpnotu vājinaḥ
ityābhāṣya dadau kanyāmarthibhaṅgabhayānnṛpaḥ
gālavastāṃ samādāya visṛjya garuḍaṃ yayau
haryaśvaṃ nāma sa nṛpaṃ vīraṃ matimatāṃ varam
uvāca rājankanyeyaṃ tvayā śulkena gṛhyatām
hayānāṃ śyāmakarṇānāṃ dehi tena nṛpātmajām
ātmajaṃ janayitvaikaṃ dāsyāmyenāṃ punastava
iti saṃvidamādāya sa tāṃ jagrāha vājibhiḥ
tatastasyāṃ sa kālena jayantamiva vāsavaḥ
putraṃ vasumanaḥsaṃjñaṃ vasuvīryamajījanat
atha tasmātsamādāya yayātitanayāṃ muniḥ
tayaiva saṃvidā prāyāddivodāsāya bhūbhuje
pratardanābhidheyasya jāte putre punarmuniḥ
samādāyāśvaśeṣārthī vrajanprāpa khagādhipam
tamabravītturaṅgānāṃ mayāptāni śatāni ṣaṭ
śeṣaṃ saṃprāptyupāye me sauhārdāccintyatāṃ tvayā
iti pṛṣṭo viṣaṇṇena muninā vinatātmajaḥ
uvāca ṣaṭ śatānyeva pṛthivyāṃ santi vājinām
sahasraṃ śyāmakarṇānāmṛcīkatapasā purā
prāptaṃ vivāhaśulkārthaṃ vāruṇaṃ hayato 'rthataḥ
kālena tāvatā teṣāṃ kasmiṃścidrājasagare
vaitastena pravāhena hṛtaṃ śatacatuṣṭayam
hayānāṃ ṣaṭśatānyeva tasmātsanti mahītale
aśvasaṃpūraṇaṃ kanyāṃ dehyenāṃ gurave sakhe
garuḍenetyabhihite gālavastāṃsturaṅgamān
dattvā kanyāṃ ca tāṃ prādādgurave tanayāvadhi
viśvāmitras tatastasyāṃ turyaṃ tanayamaṣṭakam
janayitvendrasadṛśaṃ gālavāyaiva tāṃ dadau
gālavaḥ śubhakṛtyo 'tha tanayāṃ tāṃ yayātaye
varād abhraṣṭakaumārāṃ dadau padmasamānanām
tato yayātirduhitustasyāścakre svayaṃvaram
carācarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ samāje parikalpyate
vicārya mādhavī tatra surānsiddharṣibhūmipān
viviktaṃ kānanaṃ vavre varaṃ tīrthatapodhiyā
tatra śaṣpāṅkurāhāramṛgasabrahmacāriṇī
sā cacāra paritrastā lokaśaṅkābhayādiva
yayātiratha kālena yajvā prāpya surālayam
sarvabhūtāvamānena kṣīṇapuṇyo 'pataddivaḥ
sa patanneva dauhitraiḥ svapuṇyenāṣṭakādibhiḥ
punarāropitaḥ svarge putryā ca tapasā tayā
prāptavānatinirbandhādgālavo duḥkhavikriyām
yayātiścātimānena nipapāta mahītalam
nāradeneti kathitaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ suyodhanam
kṛṣṇaśca bhīṣmadroṇau ca gāndhārī cedamūcire
duryodhanahitaṃ vākyaṃ budhyasva svakulaśriye
mā gamaḥ pārthakopāgnau mohādbālapataṅgavat
saṃdhāya pāṇḍutanayairvasudhāṃ vasudhāmabhiḥ
pravardhamānavibhavairbhuktvā kīrtimahāpayan
śrutvaitadgāḍhasaṃrambho jagāda dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ
avaśyaṃbhāvino bhāvā bhavantyevānivartinaḥ
jayo vā saṃśayo lakṣmyā vadho vā svargado yudhi
na hyekamanayoḥ pakṣamahaṃ paśyāmi nirmalam
aśikṣitapraṇāmānāṃ pṛthvīmūlyaṃ manasvinām
ta eva praṇatāḥ śatrau labhante na varāṭikām
pravṛttadarpā vairāktāḥ pāṇḍavā mānino bhuvi
sūcyagraparimāṇe 'pi kimanyanme na bhāginaḥ
ityuktvā kauravaḥ kṛṣṇagrahaṇe jātaniścayaḥ
nirgatya karṇapramukhaiḥ saṃmantrya punarāviśat
teṣāṃ tadiṅgitaṃ jñātvā sātyakirdhīmatāṃ varaḥ
nyavedayadasaṃrambhāt kṛṣṇāyākṛṣṇakarmaṇe
tataḥ kopānalajvālā jaṭābhiriva pūrayan
tāṃ sabhāṃ kaiṭabhārātirghoraṃ vapuradarśayat
sarvadevamaye tasya śarīre bhāsvaratviṣaḥ
rūpaṃ tasyogramālokya mumuhuḥ pṛthivīśvarāḥ
anantamaprameyaṃ tadviśvarūpamadhokṣajaḥ
darśayitvā munīnsarvānsamāmantrya viniryayau
rathena ghanaghoṣeṇa bhāsvadgaruḍalakṣmaṇā
vidurāvasathaṃ gatvā sa kuntīṃ draṣṭumāviśat
taṃ bhrātuḥ putramāyātaṃ pariṣvajya hariṃ pṛthā
putrāṇāṃ kuśalaṃ śrutvā babhāṣe sāśrulocanā
kṛṣṇa madvayasā vācyastvayā dharmasuto ghṛṇī
ārjavaṃ brahmasulabhaṃ na te kṣatriya śobhate
parārdhyavacano rājā yācase vibhavaṃ nijam
pāpānpāpasahāyāṃśca kiṃ na jānāsi kauravān
ajñātaparamārthānāṃ vyavahāraparāṅmukham
aṣṭākapālaviprāṇāṃ jāḍyamevaṃvidhaṃ kṣamam
vidurā svasutaṃ pūrvaṃ rājānaṃ śatrubhirjitam
uvācārambhavimukhaṃ na rājābharaṇaṃ kṣamā
kṣamate vismṛtakrodho nikāraṃ yaḥ kṛtāgasām
gaṇanāpūraṇaṃ loke sa puṃsāṃ dharmaputrakaḥ
varaṃ kaṇṭakavānvṛkṣo na śamī saralāśayā
spṛhaṇīyā varaṃ vandhyā na mātā śāntatejasām
mātrā vidurayetyuktaḥ saṃjayo nāma bhūpatiḥ
jayodyogakṛtotsāhaścakārārinibarhaṇam
gāṇḍīvadhanvā bhagavānvācyastadrakṣaṇocitam
uttejanaṃ tu bhīmasya na vīrasyopayujyate
iti bruvāṇāmāmantrya tāṃ pāṇḍutanayānprati
dārukapreritairaśvairjagāma garuḍadhvajaḥ
tasminprayāte saṃtrasto dhṛtarāṣṭro 'tha saṃjayam
papraccha cārairanviṣya caritaṃ kaiṭabhadviṣaḥ
śrutaṃ saṃjaya kaṃsāreḥ vrajato nayaśālinaḥ
kāpi mantrakathā svairaṃ rādheyena sahābhavat
ekastvaṃ dhīmatāṃ dhuryo yadi jānāsi kathyatām
iti pṛṣṭo narendreṇa saṃjayaḥ pratyabhāṣata
śrutaṃ kathayatorgūḍhaṃ karṇakeśavayormayā
anumānya muhuḥ karṇamidamūce janārdanaḥ
devena raviṇā kuntyāṃ jātastrailokyacakṣuṣā
pāṇḍostvaṃ tanayaḥ karṇaḥ kṣetrajo dharmajāgrajaḥ
tadehi kauravāṃstyaktvā sodarānpāṇḍunandanān
sahitastairvasumatīṃ bhuṅkṣva śakra ivāmaraiḥ
śrutvaitatsādaraṃ vīraḥ karṇaḥ kṛṣṇamabhāṣata
bhagavansarvamevāhaṃ jāne saṃbhavamātmanaḥ
kiṃ tu bhuktaṃ ca pītaṃ ca visrabdhaṃ yasya mandire
duryodhanasya tasyāhaṃ droheṇa suhṛdo vibhoḥ
sahasraraśmestanayaḥ karṇo 'haṃ kathamacyuta
mitradrohaparīvādakalaṅkāṃ kāmaye śriyam
kirīṭinā mayi hate bhīmena ca suyodhane
avaśyaṃ pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnāmavāpsyati yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
matkathāṃ naiva vācyo 'sau jñātvā māṃ bhrātaraṃ hi saḥ
prāpyamapyakhilaṃ rājyaṃ nijaṃ naiva labhiṣyate
asminvidhātṛvihite kṣatrakṣetrakṣaye yudhi
pārthāndrakṣyasi vaikuṇṭhavīrānvijayaśālinaḥ
bhuñjānaḥ pāyasaṃ svapne saghṛtaṃ dhavalāmbaraḥ
asthisaṃcayamārūḍho mayā dṛṣṭo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
sahasrapāde prāsāde bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ
śuddhamālyo mahotsāhaḥ sa evālokitaḥ punaḥ
atyuccagiriśṛṅgastho dṛṣṭaḥ śrīmānvṛkodaraḥ
kirīṭī tvatsahāyaśca pāṇḍuradvipamūrdhani
sānugaḥ kauravapatiḥ śoṇamālyānulepanaḥ
dakṣiṇāśāṃ vrajandṛṣṭo mayā gardabhavāhanaḥ
dṛṣṭāśca dhavaloṣṇīṣā drauṇihārdikyagautamāḥ
tānvinā dhruvamasmāsu kṛtānto vicariṣyati
dṛśyante durnimittāni yathā ghorāṇi keśava
tathā jāne na naḥ śeṣo gāṇḍīvena bhaviṣyati
iti karṇena kathite svairaṃ vinayaśālinā
taṃ samāmantrya bhagavāñjagāma garuḍadhvajaḥ
kṛṣṇe prayāte viduraḥ kuntīṃ tanayavatsalām
uvācābhyetya kuṭilaṃ duryodhanaviceṣṭitam
anunīto 'pi bahuśo mumūrṣurdhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ
asmadvaco na gṛhṇāti pathyaṃ bāla ivāturaḥ
amānite gate kṛṣṇe kurupāṇḍavasaṃgare
dhruvaṃ pravṛtte nikhilā pṛthivī na bhaviṣyati
śrutvaitadvidureṇoktaṃ kuntī cintākulāśayā
karṇaṃ japaparaṃ prāyātsthitaṃ bhāgīrathītaṭe
āpṛṣṭhatāpād udyantaṃ taṃ bhāskaramupasthitam
pratīkṣamāṇā sā tasthau prauḍhatāpaklamārditā
japānte tāṃ samālokya karṇo viracitāñjaliḥ
rādheyaḥ sūtaputro 'haṃ kiṃ karomītyabhāṣata
sā taṃ babhāṣe vātsalyāt kanīnastvaṃ suto mama
janakaste sahasrāṃśurna sūtaḥ pṛthutejasaḥ
yudhiṣṭhireṇa saṃgamya bhrātrā vinayaśālinā
bhuṅkṣva vīra mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ mā pāpānkauravānbhaja
iti mātrārthitaḥ karṇastadevodīritaṃ divaḥ
sākṣāddevena raviṇā śuśrāva vipulāśayaḥ
so 'vadatpraṇataḥ kuntīṃ mātarjāne tvayoditam
vṛddhasyādhiratheḥ kiṃtu nāsthāṃ hātumahaṃ vibhuḥ
ājanmasaṃbhṛtas tasya snehānmayi manorathaḥ
kathamekapade yāntu nīcasauhārdavadvṛthā
bahiścaraṃ jīvitaṃ ca na tyājyo mama kauravaḥ
sarvāvasthāsu yasyāhaṃ bandhuḥ svāmī guruḥ suhṛt
kasminsamaye mātastava putrānvinārjunam
na haniṣyāmi mā te 'stu praṇayo 'yaṃ vṛthā mayi
mayā hate phalgune vā hate pārthena vā mayi
pañcaputraiva bhavatī kimanyadvicariṣyati
ukte vaikartaneneti muhuḥ kampitamānasā
tamāmantrya yayau gūḍhaṃ vidurāvasathaṃ pṛthā
bhagavānatha samprāpya pāṇḍavānkaiṭabhāntakaḥ
nyavedayatkauravāṇāmabhiprāyaṃ durantaram
tato babhūva saṃrambhaḥ sattvotsāhasamuddhataḥ
senāsu pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ vijayārambhavibhramaḥ
kṛṣṇasyānumate vīraṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahābhujam
pāṇḍavāḥ pāvakājjātaṃ senāpatimakalpayat
abhiṣikte tatastasminprahṛṣṭe vipulaujasi
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kurukṣetraṃ pratasthe vipulairbalaiḥ
tasya rājasamudrasya sotsāhaṃ parisarpataḥ
nirghoṣo vāhinīsaṅghasaṃgharṣaprabhavo 'bhavat
gajavājirathoddhūtasārdradhūlīkadambakaiḥ
jvaliṣyataḥ śatruvahner dhūmotpīḍāyitaṃ puraḥ
divākarakaraspṛṣṭaratnābharaṇarociṣaḥ
vicerurbhūbhujāṃ hemanārācanicayā iva
bandibhirgīyamānāste yaśovikramalāñchanaiḥ
nāmabhirmenire vīrā devānapi na durjayān
karṇatālāniloddhūtagajasindūrareṇavaḥ
cakrire rudhirāvartapūrṇāmiva nabhastaṭīm
kurukṣetramathāsādya sakṛṣṇāḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥ
nadyāstīre hiraṇvatyā rājñāṃ sthānānyakalpayan
parikhāparirūḍhāni śibirāṇi nareśvarāḥ
kṛṣṇārjunopadiṣṭāni sādaraṃ bhejire narāḥ
saṃniviṣṭe kurukṣetre rājabhiḥ saha pāṇḍave
nanādeva mahī kliṣṭā śaṅkhadundubhiniḥsvanaiḥ
atrāntare kurupatiḥ sahasrairbhūbhujāṃ vṛtaḥ
niryayau pṛthivīṃ kurvandhvajacchatramayīmiva
sa daśaikādhikāḥ śrīmānkarṣannakṣauhiṇīrbabhau
prabhā iva sahasrāṃśuḥ saritpatirivāpagāḥ
karavālā babhustasya gajaśailākule bale
bhūpīḍitā iva vyālāḥ pātālavivarotthitāḥ
sa vilokya mahīpālāndroṇakarṇakṛpādibhiḥ
sahito 'bhyetya vinayāddevavratamabhāṣata
astu naḥ śaktimānvīraḥ kārtikeya ivāparaḥ
mahatyasminraṇārambhe vāhinīnāṃ vibhurbhavān
ityarthitaḥ kauraveṇa vyājahāra pitāmahaḥ
eṣo 'haṃ tava senānīr yotsye pāṇḍusutāniti
sadāvaropayiṣyāmi yoddhāyutavadhādapi
na cāpametadityetāṃ viddhi me yudhi saṃvidam
iti vādini gāṅgeye dhārtarāṣṭrena sādaram
abhiṣikte jagatkṛtsnaṃ cakampe sāśanisvanam
kurukṣetramathāsādya duryodhanagirā śanaiḥ
rasavanti vibhaktāni śibirāṇyabhajannṛpāḥ
śrutvā yudhiṣṭhiro bhīṣmaṃ kṛtaṃ senāpatiṃ paraiḥ
uvāca bhūmipānsarvānanujāṃśca hareḥ puraḥ
pūrvaṃ bhīṣmeṇa no yuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati mahaujasā
jambhārirapi no yasya samare gaṇanāspadam
caritaṃ vikramodāraṃ gāyanti tridaśāṅganāḥ
yattā bhavantastiṣṭhantu śakyate na sa helayā
yudhi dhairyanidhirvaktuṃ dhaureyaḥ sarvadhanvinām
ityuktvā vidadhe dhīmānkṛṣṇasyānumate nṛpaḥ
patīnsaptasu senāsu saptaśakraparākramān
mātsyadrupadaśaineyadhṛṣṭaketuśikhaṇḍinaḥ
māgadhaḥ pārṣataśceti tatsenāpatayo 'bhavan
ino babhūva teṣāṃ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnastarasvinām
tasyopari paridraṣṭā pārtho 'bhūtkṛṣṇapālitaḥ
atrāntare haladharastulyo bhīmasuyodhanau
priyau śiṣyau sadā matvā śanaistaṃ deśamāyayau
sa dharmarājamāmantrya sānujaṃ sajanārdanam
bandhuyuddhaviraktātmā draṣṭuṃ tīrthānyagātkṛtī
tasmingate samabhyāyātpāṇḍavānbhīṣmakātmajaḥ
rukmī nāma kare yasya māhendravijayaṃ dhanuḥ
akṣauhiṇyā vṛtaḥ śrīmānvijitākhilabhūmipaḥ
so 'bhyetya madasaṃrabdhaḥ savyasācinamabravīt
karomi tava sāhāyyaṃ samare 'sminviśaṅkaṭe
bhīṣmadroṇau haniṣyāmi yadi bhīto 'si phalguna
śrutvaitadarjuno 'vādīd asaṃrambhaḥ smitottaram
bata bhītaparitrātā paribhrāmyasi bhūtale
nivātakavacocchede gandharvavijaye 'pi vā
gograhe vā sakhā kaścitko bhavenme bhavadvidhaḥ
yathāgataṃ vrajetyuktaḥ sa sāvajñaṃ kirīṭinā
tadeva gatvā darpāndho duryodhanamabhāṣata
tenāpi māninā tyaktaḥ sa jagāma nijāṃ purīm
tasminprayāte balayorārambho vipulo 'bhavat
asmin avasare rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sutapriyaḥ
papraccha saṃjayaṃ ceṣṭāṃ kurupāṇḍavasenayoḥ
sa tena pṛṣṭaḥ provāca saṃniviṣṭe baladvaye
ulūkaṃ śakuneḥ sūnumādideśa suyodhanaḥ
gaccha kauravya kaunteyaṃ brūhi bhūmipālasaṃsadi
mā vilambasva samare dīrghadīrghaparāśrayaḥ
iṣṭebhyo dattasarvasvaḥ kuruṣva priyasaṃgamān
upasthitaṃ nātidūrādyuddhaṃ śāntanavena vaḥ
iti duryodhanenokto gatvā saubalasaṃbhavaḥ
tadevovāca bhūpālamadhye bhīmārjunāgrajam
tamūcatuḥ krudhā tāmranetrau kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau
ulūka kālapakvo 'sau prātardraṣṭā suyodhanaḥ
manyate yaśca gāṅgeyaṃ samare 'sminparāyaṇam
tameva drakṣyati śaraiśchinnaṃ gāṇḍīvanirgataiḥ
iti pratisamādiṣṭastābhyāṃ gāndhāranandanaḥ
gatvā taddhārtarāṣṭrāya rājamadhye nyavedayat
suyodhanena pṛṣṭo 'tha rathasaṃkhyāṃ pitāmahaḥ
uvāca kalpayanvīravaktreṣu pulakaśriyam
śṛṇu senāniveśe 'sminpareṣāmātmanastathā
saṃgame sarvavīrāṇāṃ mahāratharathāntaram
pravarastvaṃ ratho rājanbhrātṛbhiḥ sahito rathaiḥ
ātmanaśca guṇānvaktuṃ pragalbhante na mādṛśaḥ
hārdikyo 'tiratho vīro madrarājaśca tatsamaḥ
bhūriśravā rathāgryāṇāṃ pravaro yūthapādhipaḥ
rathaḥ sudakṣiṇo rājā saindhavo dviguṇo rathaḥ
vindānuvindau nīlaśca prakhyātāḥ syandanottamāḥ
suśarmā sānujo vīro ratho vīrataro mama
lakṣmaṇastava putraśca bhrātā duḥśāsanaśca te
khyātau rathottamau vīrau daṇḍadhāraśca bhūpatiḥ
rathottamau mahāvīrānugrāyudhabṛhadbalau
śāradvataḥ kṛpo vīro yūthapānāṃ tu yūthapaḥ
ratho gāndhāranṛpatiḥ śakunirmātulastava
rudrasya tejasā yukto drauṇiḥ śataguṇo rathaḥ
droṇaśca rathayūthānāṃ praṇetā triguṇo rathaḥ
satyaśravā rathodāro vṛṣaseno mahārathaḥ
jalasaṃdho rathavaro māgadho 'tirathaḥ smṛtaḥ
bāhlikastatsamo vīraḥ satyamān uttamo rathaḥ
alabuṣo rākṣasendraḥ prakhyāto rathasattamaḥ
prāgjyotiṣo bahuguṇo bhagadatto rathādhipaḥ
ratho gāndhāratanayau bhrātarau vṛṣakācalau
ghṛṇī prasādanirato varmakuṇḍalavarjitaḥ
puruṣaḥ katthano nīcaḥ karṇa eva rathottamaḥ
śrutvaitatkrodhatāmrākṣaḥ karṇo nāga ivāśvasan
uvāca bata vṛddho 'pi bhīṣma bālāyase dhiyā
mohādakāraṇadveṣāddarpādvā marmadāraṇam
satataṃ pāpa kaṭukaṃ bhāṣamāṇo na lajjase
upasthiteṣu yuddheṣu mahatsu nayavedibhiḥ
api mithyāstutipadaiḥ kriyante bhīravo bhaṭāḥ
voḍhavye rājakārye 'sminmahatāṃ yadvimānanam
kuruṣe tadahaṃ jāne parairnyasto 'si bhedakaḥ
na taccitramidaṃ manye rathasaṃkhyā yaducyate
śauryaṃ tejaśca śūrāṇāṃ vacasā gaṇyate katham
yadi duryodhano rājā sahate kāryagauravāt
tadasmākaṃ kimāyātaṃ nyakkāraṃ yatkṣamāmahe
ahaṃ jeṣyāmi pārthānāṃ vipulaṃ balamāgatam
uccaiḥ kṛto 'si mithyaiva kiṃ kurmo bhīṣma bhūbhujā
mayā jite 'thavā śatrau yaśastvā pratipadyate
ahate tvayi gāṅgeya tasmādyotsye na pāṇḍavaiḥ
ityukte sūtaputreṇa vīraḥ śāntanavo 'bravīt
viśrānte yudhyamāne vā kā nāmāsyā raṇe tvayi
asmin upasthite kārye rājñaḥ suciracintite
bhedaḥ saṃrakṣyate 'smābhiryena karṇa na hanyase
iti bruvankauraveṇa pṛṣṭaḥ śāntanavaḥ punaḥ
uvāca pāṇḍavabale rathānāṃ sāraphalgutām
svayaṃ yudhiṣṭhiro rājā yamau ca balināṃ varau
mahārathā mahotsāhāścariṣyanti bale tava
rathastvaṣṭaguṇo bhīmaḥ śūro rathaśatādhipaḥ
viditaḥ sarvavīrāṇāṃ yādṛśaḥ phalguno rathaḥ
draupadeyā rathāḥ pañca tathā vairāṭiruttaraḥ
abhimanyuḥ pitustulyo devasya ca suradviṣaḥ
pravaro rathayūthānāṃ sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
rathau mama matau vīrau yudhāmanyūttamaujasau
virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau dṛṣṭasārau mahārathau
dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca khyātāvatirathau bhuvi
kṛtavarmā tvardharatho dhṛṣṭadyumnasutaḥ śiśuḥ
dhṛṣṭaketuḥ kṣatradevo jayantaś citrajijjayaḥ
kuntibhojaścekitānaḥ pañca vīrāśca kekayāḥ
śaibyaśca kāśirājaśca matāḥ sarve rathottamāḥ
śaṅkhādayo matsyaputrā vārakṣemaśca bhūpatiḥ
citrāyudhaḥ satyadhṛtiḥ senābinduśca pauravaḥ
purajiccandrasenaśca śreṇimāṃśca mahārathāḥ
rocamānaśca tattulyo vasudānaśca sātmajaḥ
draupadaḥ satyajidvīro mato me 'ṣṭaguṇo rathaḥ
ghaṭotkaco bahuguṇo yūthapapravaro rathaḥ
anye tvardharathā vīrāḥ pārthivāḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥ
etānsarvānahaṃ yotsye guptāngāṇḍīvadhanvanā
apyudyatāstraḥ strīrūpamekaṃ muktvā śikhaṇḍinam
purā vicitravīryasya bhrāturarthe mayā puraḥ
rājño hṛtāḥ kāśipatestisraḥ kanyāḥ svayaṃvare
ambāmbikāmbālikā ca tā narendra pramāthinaḥ
rathe me yudhyamānasya latā iva cakampire
prasthitaṃ māṃ tato dṛṣṭvā nirjitāśeṣabhūmipam
uvācāmbābhidhā jyeṣṭhā tāsāṃ kamalalocanā
sālvarājo mayā pūrvaṃ manasā dayito vṛtaḥ
nākāmāmabalāṃ vīra balānmā hartumarhasi
etadākarṇya sahasā tāmahaṃ jvalitāmiva
atyajaṃ bhāratakule kalaṅkaparihāradhīḥ
sā gatvā sālvanṛpatiṃ saṃkalpaṃ vinivedya tam
uvāca bhaja māṃ nātha praṇayātsvayamāgatām
ityukto mṛgaśāvākṣyā tayā sālvamahīpatiḥ
hṛtānyeneti tāṃ mānī na jagrāha kulodgataḥ
sā daivādubhayabhraṣṭā gatvā duḥkhāttapovanam
munīnyayāce pravrajyāṃ svavṛttāntaṃ nivedya tam
tasyā evātha rājarṣistatra mātāmahaḥ sthitaḥ
viṣaṇṇastatkathāṃ śrutvā babhāṣe hotravāhanaḥ
mahendraparvate putri rāmo bhṛgukulodvahaḥ
vartate karuṇāsindhurgaccha taṃ śaraṇaṃ vibhum
śiṣyo hi tasya vacasā guroḥ śantanunandanaḥ
grahīṣyati parityaktāmapi tvāṃ mā śucaṃ kṛthāḥ
ityukte jāmadagnyasya jyeṣṭhaḥ śiṣyaḥ kṛtavrataḥ
yadṛcchayā samabhyāyāttaṃ deśaṃ munisevitam
sa śrutvā pūjitaḥ kanyākathāṃ tāṃ hotravāhinīm
uvāca prātarāgantā rāmaḥ svayamidaṃ vanam
ukte kṛtavrateneti tasminyāte 'tha vāsare
prātaḥ śrīmānsvayaṃ rāmo bhāsvaraḥ pratyadṛśyata
taṃ pūjitaṃ munivaraiḥ praṇamyālaṃkṛtāsanam
rājaputrī kṛpāsindhuṃ sabāṣpā śaraṇaṃ yayau
tasyā vṛttāntamākarṇya so 'vadatsaralāśayaḥ
putri madvacasā bhīṣmo na tvāṃ tyakṣyati gauravāt
eṣo 'haṃ kauravakṣetraṃ gatvā śāntanavaṃ svayam
anuśāsya vidhāsyāmi dakṣiṇaṃ tvatsamīhite
ityuktvā śiṣyasahitastāṃ samādāya bhārgavaḥ
kurukṣetraṃ yayau tejaḥpuñjairāpūrayandiśaḥ
sākṣādabhyāgataṃ jñātvā muniṃ mānyaṃ divaukasām
pratyudgato 'haṃ sahasā puraskṛtya purodhasam
rāmo māmāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā pūjāmādāya sānugaḥ
uvāca bhīṣma kanyeyaṃ hṛtā tyaktā ca kiṃ tvayā
tvadvisṛṣṭā parityaktā sālvenāpi durātmanā
gṛhāṇaināṃ mama girā bhrāturarthe manasvinīm
etadgurorniśamyāhaṃ vacanaṃ karuṇānidheḥ
avadaṃ naḥ kule neyamucitā bhāvadūṣitā
svayaṃ yātāṃ sālvapatiṃ tena tyaktāṃ ca madbhayāt
kathaṃ kulakalaṅkāya gṛhṇāmyenāṃ bhavadgirā
prasīda bhagavannaitadvaktumarhasyasāṃpratam
mayetyabhihito rāmaḥ kopādākulito 'vadat
śiṣyo bhūtvā kathaṃ bhīṣma mohānmāmavamanyase
upasthito vināśaste madājñābhaṅgakāriṇaḥ
aho bata na jānīṣe navarājanyavaṃśajaḥ
triḥ saptakṛtvaḥ kṣapitakṣatraṃ mā hehayāntakam
ityahaṃ tadvacaḥ śrutvā punaḥ punarudīritam
avocaṃ kiṃcid udbhinnakopasvedārdravigrahaḥ
upadeṣṭā satāṃ vṛtte gururityucyate budhaiḥ
sa evotpathamāpannaḥ parityājya iti śrutiḥ
sa tvaṃ dharmādapete 'rthe mā niyoktumihodyataḥ
arho 'si mama bāṇāgre kṣatriyācārasaṃgare
aśūrāste purā sarve nihatāḥ kṣatriyāstvayā
manye 'haṃ jātavānkaścinna tadā mādṛśo janaḥ
yatheṣṭaṃ vīra yudhyasva śiṣyairanugato nṛpaiḥ
cāpadvitīyaḥ sajjo 'haṃ tvaddarpocchittaye yataḥ
mayetyukte gururgarvāt tejasvī bhṛgunandanaḥ
udatiṣṭhatkurukṣetre vīraḥ samarasaṃmukhaḥ
tasmindivyarathārūḍhe dīptāstre bhāsuratviṣi
yuyutsuṃ jāhnavī devī mātābhyetya jagāda mām
kṣatrakandāgninā putra mā kṛthā bhṛgusūnunā
virodhaṃ yāvadenaṃ te prasādamahamarthaye
iti mātrāpyabhihito nātyajaṃ svakulavratam
vīrā bhayapraṇāmeṣu bharatā na hi śikṣitāḥ
kṛṣṭacāpaṃ praṇamyāhaṃ taṃ guruṃ sarvadhanvinām
tatpūrvaśarapātārthī muhūrtaṃ niścalo 'bhavam
tatastadastravalayajvālāvalayitāmbare
agamaṃ śarasaṅghānāṃ madhye kṣaṇamadṛśyatām
athāha śaṅkhanādena paripūrya diśo daśa
ayodhayaṃ raṇe rāmaṃ virāmaṃ kṣatratejasām
tena me yudhyamānasya niṣkampasya dinatrayam
apūjayansurāḥ sarve vikramaṃ puṣpavarṣiṇaḥ
vasubhirbrāhmaṇākārairjāhnavyā ca muhurmuhuḥ
dhṛto 'haṃ jāmadagnyāstrapātamūrchitamānasaḥ
tato mahāstranivahairahaṃ śiṣyaṃ pinākinaḥ
nirjitya bhārgavaṃ yatnādyuddhe ślathamanoratham
tasmātsamarasaṃmardādvirato vismito 'tha saḥ
kāśirājasutāmūce kiṃcidābhugnakandharaḥ
durjayo yudhi gāṅgeyaḥ kiṃ karomi nṛpātmaje
kṣatrajātiratikrūrā guruṃ māṃ nābhimanyate
adhunā kṣattriyaḥ śiṣyo mayā varjya iti bruvan
mahendraṃ prayayau rāmaḥ svapuraṃ cāhamāviśam
tataḥ kāśipateḥ putrī manyuduḥkhānalākulā
āśrameṣu maharṣīṇāṃ cakre ghorataraṃ tapaḥ
bhūyānmānavihīnāyā janma bhīṣmavadhāya me
ityāśayā sā tīrtheṣu nirāhārā śanairabhūt
dṛṣṭvā tīvratapaḥkṣāmāṃ tāmuvāca surāpagā
dehānte kuṭilācārā vatsadeśe bhaviṣyasi
tumbīti taṭinī khyātā ghorasattvaniṣevitā
ityuktā svargasaritā kālena vṛṣabhadhvajam
niyatārādhya varadaṃ varaṃ prāpa manogatam
putrārthinaḥ sā kālena rājño raudratapojuṣaḥ
ajāyata sutāṃ pūrvaṃ drupadasyeśvarecchayā
bhāvī pumānasau kanyā bhagavānityabhāṣata
yasmāttasmānnṛpastasyāḥ khyāpayāmāsa putratām
śikhaṇḍītikṛtābhikhyaḥ sā kanyā kūṭaputrakaḥ
dāśārṇādhipateḥ putrīṃ bhāryāṃ lebhe sulocanām
sā yauvanavatī dṛṣṭvā śayyāyāṃ tāṃ śikhaṇḍinīm
striyaṃ duḥkhārditā pitre dūtyā sarvaṃ nyavedayat
vitīrṇāṃ kūṭaputrāya sutāṃ dāśārṇabhūpatiḥ
hiraṇyavarmā vijñāya drupadaṃ yoddhumāyayau
tasminsuvipulānīke pratyāsanne tarasvini
drupadaścintayāviṣṭo na lebhe kāryaniścayam
viṣaṇṇaṃ pitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā mātaraṃ ca śikhaṇḍinī
ātmānaṃ kāraṇaṃ matvā yayāvekākinī vanam
sā śokārtā nirāhārā sthūṇākarṇena pālitā
tasminvane mahadveśma dadarśa maṇiveṣṭitam
praviśya sahasā tasthau nirāhārā ciraṃ śucā
yakṣaśca vīkṣya tāṃ śrutvā tadvṛttāntamabhāṣata
puruṣavyañjanaṃ prāpya mayā dattaṃ sumadhyame
gatvā trāyasva pitaraṃ nijaṃ rūpaṃ prayaccha me
kṛtakāryā ca na cirātpunaryoṣā bhaviṣyasi
iti saṃvidamādāya visṛṣṭā tena sā yayau
dattaṃ vinimayāttena sā rūpaṃ prāpya pauruṣam
pitre svapuramāsādya vṛttāntaṃ svaṃ nyavedayat
hṛṣṭo jāmātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā dāśārṇaḥ prītiśālinam
āmantrya drupadaṃ prāyādvitīrya draviṇaṃ bahu
atrāntare dhanapatiḥ sthūṇākarṇagṛhaṃ svayam
yāto dadarśa strīrūpaṃ taṃ hriyā nodgataṃ puraḥ
tato viditavṛttāntaḥ kuberastamabhāṣata
strīrūpa eva pāpa tvaṃ narastvastu śikhaṇḍinī
tajjīvāvadhi madvākyādityastu vyatyayaściram
abhidhāyeti kupite yāte vaiśravaṇe svayam
kṛtakṛtyastamabhyāyādyakṣaṃ drupadanandanaḥ
dātuṃ prāptaṃ nijaṃ rūpaṃ satyavādinamārjavāt
dṛṣṭvā śikhaṇḍinaṃ yakṣo viṣaṇṇavadano 'vadat
gaccha pāñcālya nedaṃ me strīrūpaṃ yujyate svayam
tyaktaṃ śāpāddhanapatermadrūpaṃ tvaṃ ca rakṣitā
iti yakṣavacaḥ śrutvā śikhaṇḍī svapuraṃ yayau
sarvāstraśastrakuśalo yakṣatulyaparākramaḥ
evaṃ na strī na puruṣaḥ strīpūrvo drupadātmajaḥ
varjyo yudhi mayā nityamiti me kṣatriyavratam
palāyamāne nyastāstre muktakeśe vivarmaṇi
strīpūrve śaraṇaṃ yāte na śūraḥ śantanoḥ sutaḥ
niśāyāmityabhihite bhīṣmeṇa nṛpasaṃsadi
duryodhano 'vadatprātaḥ praṇipatya pitāmaham
kālena kiyatā sainyaṃ pāṇḍūnāṃ sāgaropamam
śaktaḥ kṣapayituṃ kiṃ vā droṇaḥ karṇaḥ kṛpo 'thavā
ityuktaḥ kururājena hasañśāntanavo 'bravīt
mahāstradarśī satataṃ hantu māsena tadbalam
śakto'hamiti tenokte tadeva gururabhyadhāt
kṛpo māsadvayeneti drauṇiśca daśabhirdinaiḥ
pañcabhirdivasaiḥ karṇaḥ pratijajñe ripukṣayam
tato vihasya sotprāśaṃ bhīṣmaḥ karṇaṃ vigarhayan
nābhyanandatpṛthubalaṃ kathayansavyasācinam
atrāntare dharmasuto babhāṣe śvetavāhanam
apārāḥ pārtha manye 'haṃ kururājavarūthinīḥ
kālena kiyatā tāsāṃ kṣayaṃ phalguṇa manyase
iti pṛṣṭo nṛpatinā babhāṣe śakranandanaḥ
yoddhāhaṃ sārathiḥ kṛṣṇo gāṇḍīvaṃ dhanurūrjitam
astraṃ pāśupataṃ ghoraṃ priyaṃ devasya dhūrjaṭeḥ
āsthā kā tatra martyeṣu yatraitattulyamudyatam
ityuktavati kaunteye praharṣādbhujaśālinām
babhūvurvigrahā rājñāṃ spaṣṭaromāñcakañcukāḥ
asminkṣaṇe nṛpagirā kṛpasaumadattimadrādhināthabhagadattajayadrathādyāḥ
agresaraṃ tripathagātanayaṃ vidhāya yuddhāṅgaṇaṃ viviśurāśu vimuktadhāma
puṇye bhārgavabhinnabhūpanidhane kṣetre tataḥ kaurave kaunteyasya samantapañcakataṭe senāniveśo babhau
tvaṅgattuṅgaturaṅgakuñjaraghaṭāvyālolitakṣmātaṭīghṛṣṭavyākulaśeṣamastakamaṇijvālānibhair āyudhaiḥ
karṇāṭāśvakarūṣikādhipatayo matsyāṅgavaṅgādhipāḥ śailāḥ saindhavasālvamālavaśakaprāgjyotiṣakṣmādharāḥ
suhmakrāthakirātacīnayavanā gauḍetraparyantajāḥ kṛcchreṇa kṣitipālalakṣanibiḍaṃ tatrāntaraṃ lebhire
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam
devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet
āsūryakiraṇākrāntājjagato janagocarāt
puṇyadhāmni kurukṣetre samāyāteṣu rājasu
ekībhūteṣu sainyeṣu kurupāṇḍavasaṃgare
vṛddhabālāvaśeṣāsu dikṣu yātāsu śūnyatām
dāruṇeṣu nimitteṣu prādurbhūteṣu sarvataḥ
mitho dṛṣṭipathaṃ yāte patākābhirbaladvaye
sotsāhaṃ dadhmatuḥ śaṅkhaṃ hṛṣīkeśadhanaṃjayau
yayorgambhīraghoṣeṇa bhuvanāni cakampire
viṣamastho na hantavyo na ca senāvinirgataḥ
na nivṛtte raṇe ceti maryādāṃ cakrire nṛpāḥ
atrāntare samabhyetya pārāśaryo munīśvaraḥ
viṣaṇṇaṃ mandiragataṃ dhṛtarāṣṭramabhāṣata
vīrāṇāṃ bhūmipālānāmaśeṣe 'sminsamāgame
kṣatrasya saṃkṣayo rājanviṣamaḥ samupasthitaḥ
divyaṃ gṛhāṇa nayanaṃ svayaṃ yuddhaṃ vilokaya
ityukte muninā rājā jagādākulitāśayaḥ
bhagavānbandhunidhanaṃ nāhaṃ draṣṭuṃ samutsahe
bhāvyasyāvaśyabhāvitvānna ca vārayituṃ kṣamaḥ
ityuktavati bhūpāle saṃjayaṃ varado muniḥ
vidhāya divyanayanaṃ punaḥ kṣitipamabhyadhāt
ayaṃ te nikhilaṃ yuddhaṃ kathayiṣyati saṃjayaḥ
nāsya kiṃcidavijñātaṃ divyadṛṣṭerbhaviṣyati
kṛtānto jṛmbhate rājñāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭra tavānayāt
dṛśyante durnimittāni kṣayakarṇejapāni yat
saureṇa pīḍitā gāḍhaṃ rohiṇī jvalitā diśaḥ
viparītā prasūtiśca kabandhenāvṛto raviḥ
kravyādairāvṛtaṃ vyoma meghā varṣanti śoṇitam
kimanyadrājamahiṣī hā mahī na bhaviṣyati
pradakṣiṇaśikho vahniḥ prasādo manasastathā
lakṣavyaktaṃ jayasyaitaddharmo yatrāsti tatra saḥ
śatānyekena jīyante naiko jeyaḥ śatairapi
taralā hyasidhāreyaṃ niścayo nātra gaṇyate
ityuktvāntarhite kṣipraṃ munīndre saṃjayaṃ nṛpaḥ
papraccha dvīpasaṃsthānaṃ sa ca pṛṣṭho 'bhyabhāṣata
rājanviśāle śītāṃśormaṇḍale darpaṇākṛtau
sphāraṃ sudarśanaṃ dvīpaṃ nikhilaṃ pratibimbitam
ekataḥ pippalācchāyam anyataḥ śaśakākṛti
dvīpe 'smin maṇḍalākāre lavaṇāmbudhiveṣṭite
karṇikevāmbuje prāṃśurmadhye kanakaparvataḥ
śayānā bhūdharāścānye pārśvayostasya bhūbhṛtaḥ
sthitā himālayamukhāḥ spṛśantaḥ pūrvapaścimam
himavānhemakūṭaśca niṣadaśceti dakṣiṇe
uttare śṛṅgavānnīlaḥ śvetaśceti mahābalāḥ
eṣāṃ ratnavicitrāṇām antare varṣabhūmayaḥ
karmabhūrbhārataṃ varṣamanyāśca phalabhūmayaḥ
harivarṣamukheṣveva prajāsargaḥ smaropamaḥ
sthānaṃ sukṛtināṃ yatra vikhyātā gaṇḍikā iti
jambūkhaṇḍaṃ tathā meroradho yatphalavisrutā
jātā jambūnadī śubhrā jāmbunadavidhāyinī
uttarāḥ kuravaḥ pītvā tāmeva gatamṛtyavaḥ
divaspṛśastarestasya nāmnedaṃ dvīpamucyate
ityuktvā saṃjayo gatvā kurukṣetre raṇāṅgaṇe
sametya dhṛtarāṣṭrāya śaśaṃsa svabhaṭakṣayam
śṛṇu rājanhatānantasāmantaḥ śantanoḥ sutaḥ
vidadhe pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ yathā vijayasaṃśayam
vajrasūcīmukhākhyābhyāṃ vyūhābhyāṃ rājakuñjaraiḥ
mitho vyūḍheṣvanīkeṣu gāṅgeyenārjunena ca
tasminkṣattrakṣayakṣetre sarvakṣattrasamāgame
duryodhane 'tisaṃrabdhe pṛthusainyābhimānini
gāṅgeyaśaṅkhanādena samudbhūte balārṇave
śaṅkhaśabdena pārthānāṃ pāñcajanyānuyāyinā
pūrite bhuvanābhoge dikṣu visphūrjitāsviva
sarvasenāśrayaḥ śrīmānvijayo 'cyutasārathiḥ
dadarśa kurusenāsu gurusaṃbandhibāndhavān
nijapratāpadahane sa teṣāṃ śalabhāyitam
matvā jagāda govindaṃ viṣaṇṇaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ
aho bata vimūḍhānāṃ rājyaleśe sukhāya naḥ
kṛṣṇa bandhuvadhe 'pyasminsasaṃrambho 'yamudyamaḥ
avatīrya sadācārastutikramyakulasthitim
kathaṃ guruvadhaprāpyāṃ bhajedasmadvidhaḥ śriyam
ityuktvā sāsrunayano bībhatsuḥ kṛpayā rathe
karādutsṛjya gāṇḍīvaṃ niṣasāda viṣādavān
taṃ dṛṣṭvā śokavivaśaṃ jagāda madhusūdanaḥ
akāṇḍe dhairyasārasya keyaṃ kātaratā tava
tarasvī kṣatriyo mānī prāṇairapi yaśaḥkrayī
nijāṃ kulasthitiṃ pārtha na dharmyāṃ hātumarhasi
saṃyuktaṃ vā viyuktaṃ vā nityaṃ dehena dehinam
viśvamāyāprapañce 'sminko 'nuśocati tattvadhīḥ
sukhādyavasthā dehasya kāle kāle yathāvidhāḥ
dehino 'sya tathā dehāḥ sataḥ sattāvivarjitāḥ
viṣayendriyasaṃyogānkṣayino harṣaśokadān
sahate yo viluptātmā nirvāṇaṃ tasya śāśvatam
ajasya purāṇasya dehino 'syāvināśinaḥ
jīrṇaparṇaparāvṛttitulyeyaṃ dehakalpanā
ādimadhyāvasāneṣu vyaktāvyaktasvarūpiṇaḥ
sata evāsya satataṃ na virāmaḥ śarīriṇaḥ
ayaśasyamatastyaktvā saṃkocaṃ vipulāśayaḥ
jayājayau samaṃ matvā viśa svargonmukho raṇam
āsthāya yaugikīṃ buddhiṃ karmabandhavivarjitaḥ
śuṣkavedakriyāhīnaṃ guṇātītaṃ padaṃ bhuja
sarvavedeṣu viduṣāmetadeva prayojanam
jalāśayeṣu pūrṇeṣu yathā salilahāriṇām
niḥsaṅgaḥ phalasaṃnyāsī kuru karma sadoditaḥ
parameśvaramevāhivāṇijyaṃ hi phalārthinām
yadā te vītamohasya buddhiryāsyati nirvṛtim
kṛtī bhaviṣyasi tadā śruteṣvartheṣvanādaraḥ
iti bruvāṇaḥ pārthena sthitaprajñasya lakṣaṇam
pṛṣṭaḥ samādhisaktasya bhagavānityabhāṣata
īśvarādaparo nāhamiti svānandanirbharaḥ
nirastākhilasaṃkalpaḥ sthitaprajño 'bhidhīyate
āste kūrma ivāṅgāni kāmānsaṃvṛtyayaḥ śrayam
viṣayādhyānavirahātsthitadhīrna sa naśyati
kaṣṭaistapobhirviṣayāḥ śuṣyantyeva rasaṃ vinā
anādaraviraktānāṃ sadāpyadhyātmadarśinām
nidrālurbhūtakāleṣu prabuddhastimireṣu yaḥ
sa mahābdhirivākṣobhyaḥ sthitiṃ brāhmīṃ prapadyate
śrutvaitadarjunaḥ kṛṣṇamuvācākulitāśayaḥ
kathamevaṃ vadanghore samare 'sminyunakṣi mām
karmaṇaḥ śreyasī buddhirityuktvāpi svayaṃ vibho
karma durmatiyogyaṃ māṃ praśaṃsasi vimohayan
śreyo vadetyuktavati śvetāśve keśavo 'bravīt
niṣṭhā prajñānakarmabhyāṃ mayoktā sāṃkhyayogayoḥ
anārambhānna ca tyāgātkarmaṇo mucyate janaḥ
śrotrādayo balādasya dhāvantyeva svakarmasu
smaranti manasā sarvaṃ ruddhakarmendriyā api
mithyācārānatvasaktāḥ karmiṇo niyatāntarāḥ
śreyo hyakarmaṇaḥ karma na yajñaḥ karmaṇā vinā
yajñaśeṣāśinaḥ puṇyadrumāḥ kevalabhoginaḥ
karmasthito 'pi niḥsaṃjño yadā prāpnoti mānavaḥ
ātmārāmadaśāstuṣṭhas tadā kāryānnivartate
karmaṇaiva gatāḥ siddhiṃ janakapramukhāḥ purā
tanmā kāryānnivartasva lokastvāmanuvartatām
mamāpi kṛtakṛtyasya karmedaṃ sthitirakṣiṇaḥ
vinaśyatyanyathā loko matpramāṇaviśṛṅkhalaḥ
pātraṃ sarvajñayogyeṣu nādareṣu pṛthagjanaḥ
tasmānnotsāhayedetānpaṅgūnvegagatāniva
yudhyasva sarvakarmāṇi mayi saṃnyasya nirvṛtaḥ
taranti hi tamo ghoraṃ nityaṃ manmatavartinaḥ
prakṛterucitaṃ sarvaṃ svadharmanirataḥ kuru
rāgadveṣau parityajya priyāpriyasamudbhavau
śrutvaitadarjuno 'vādītpreritaḥ kena pātakam
caratyanīśvaraḥ prāṇī balādiva vaśīkṛtaḥ
iti pṛṣṭo hṛṣīkeśo jagāda jagatāṃ patiḥ
rajoguṇasamutthena harṣaśokādidāyinā
lokasaṃhāraśīlena kāmena krodhabandhunā
ahaṃkāreṇa balinā ghoreṇānena vairiṇā
śevālenaiva salilaṃ rajasevāmalaṃ nabhaḥ
āvṛto malinenātmā meghenaivodito raviḥ
manobuddhisamāyuktaṃ sthānamindriyapañjaram
yasya taṃ duḥsahaṃ śatruṃ kāmarūpa vināśaya
sūryeṇāptaḥ purā matto yogo 'yaṃ manunā tataḥ
ya eva kālenotsannastubhyamadya mayoditaḥ
anekajanmasākṣī tvaṃ bhaktaḥ sahacaro 'pi me
na tatsmṛtipathaṃ yātaṃ kiṃtu te prāktanaṃ vapuḥ
ahaṃ tu nityadharmasya sthitaye guptaye satām
yuge yuge bhavāmyeṣa vināśāya durātmanām
akṛtaṃ dharmakartāraṃ karmaitannāvṛṇoti mām
tvamapyasakto niṣkāmaḥ kuru karma kulocitam
durjñeyaḥ pravibhāgastu karmākarmavikarmaṇām
svocitaṃ phalahīnaṃ ca viruddhaṃ ceti bhedataḥ
karmaṇaḥ phalasaṃnyāsādyo 'nupaśyatyakarmatām
jānātyakarmaṇaḥ pāpātkarma yaśca sa buddhimān
jñānāgninā dagdhakarmā nityānando nirāśrayaḥ
nirāśīrnirahaṃkāro yajvā brahmaṇi līyate
brahmārpaṇena brahmāgnau hutvā brahmamayaṃ haviḥ
prāṇayajñarato yāti brahma brahmasamādhinā
saṃyamāgnāvindriyāṇi viṣayānindriyānale
tatkarmāṇyātmayogāgnau hutvā yānti parāṃ gatim
ye 'pi dravyatapoyogasvādhyāyajñānayājinaḥ
prāṇāpānādiha viṣo dhṛtvā nāḍīṣu dhāraṇam
samarpayanti nikhilaṃ jñānaṃ vigatakalmaṣāḥ
te prayānti paraṃ dhāma yajñaśiṣṭāmṛtāśinaḥ
tadvidhāḥ praṇipātena sevitā jñāninastvayā
ayatnāttvāṃ vidhāsyanti svātmanyakhiladarśinam
jñānāgninā dagdhapāpaḥ pavitreṇa bhaviṣyasi
kālena śraddadhānānāṃ svayaṃ jñānaṃ prasīdati
naśyanti saṃśayajuṣo mūḍhā na tvastasaṃśayāḥ
jñāninaḥ saṃśayaṃ tvasmātsthitvottiṣṭha vibhūtaye
niśamya tatpunaḥ pārthaḥ papraccha madhusūdanam
saṃnyāsakarmayogābhyāṃ śreyo brūhi janārdana
iti pṛṣṭo 'vadacchaurirubhāvetau vimuktaye
karmayogastu saṃnyāsādviśiṣṭa iti me matiḥ
śṛṇvanto 'pi vadanto 'pi spṛśanto 'pi svakarmaṇi
saktā api na sajanti paṅke ravikarā iva
tadeva vihitaṃ kiṃcitpuṃsāṃ sukṛtaduṣkṛtam
ajñānapihite jñāne kiṃ tveṣā karmavāsanā
jñānenotsāritājñānāḥ parāṃ niṣṭhāmupāgatāḥ
brāhmaṇe vā śvapāke vā vibudhāḥ samadṛṣṭayaḥ
bāhye sukhe viraktānāṃ duḥkhajanmani naśvare
antaḥsukhārāmatayā paraṃ jyotiḥ prasīdati
bahiḥ sparśānsamutsṛjya bhrūmadhyanihitekṣaṇaḥ
nāsāntare samau dhṛtvā prāṇāpānau vimuktaye
kāmarāgamadadveṣabhayakrodhavivarjitaḥ
ahantā jñānatamasāṃ śāntiṃ vindatyamatsaraḥ
kriyāvān aphalākāṅkṣī nijaṃ karma karoti yaḥ
ārurukṣudaśātīto yogārūḍho vimatsaraḥ
kūṭastho jñānatṛptaśca paśyatyātmānamātmanā
samāsanaḥ samākāro nistaraṅga ivodadhiḥ
ghrāṇāgradarśī śāntātmā māmupaiti samādhinā
yuktāhārādiceṣṭasya nityaṃ niṣkampacetasaḥ
ātmalābho bhavatyeva tyaktakāmasya yoginaḥ
manaḥ saṃyamya paśyanti sravatyetadyato yataḥ
ātmānaṃ māṃ ca sarvatra mamātmani tathākhilam
manasaścañcalasyāsya vairāgyeṇaiva saṃyamaḥ
tathābhyāsena balinā vātasyeva pramāthinaḥ
etadākarṇya kaunteyaḥ punaḥ papraccha keśavam
lolatvānmanaso deva yogādbhraṣṭasya kā gatiḥ
arjuneneti bhagavānpunaḥ pṛṣṭo 'bhyabhāṣata
yogabhraṣṭo 'pi puruṣaḥ śubhakṛttu bhaviṣyati
ciraṃ bhuktvā sukhaṃ divyaṃ sa kalyāṇapuraḥsaraḥ
bhogināṃ yogināṃ vāpi sambhūto mahatāṃ kule
pūrvābhyastaṃ punardhīmāñjanmabhiḥ pratipadyate
tapo jñānādhikaṃ yogaṃ tasmādyogī bhavārjuna
mayi nyastamanā nityaṃ bhaktyā māṃ vetti mānava
aṣṭamūrtirahaṃ sarvaṃ jīvabhūtaścarācare
utpattisthitisaṃhārakāraṇaṃ māṃ vidurbudhāḥ
sarve matprāṇitā bhāvā mayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
devīṃ māyāṃ dadhānaṃ māṃ na jānāti vimohitaḥ
ye tu jānanti māṃ māyāṃ bhavanti kṛtinaḥ sadā
arthī jijñāsurārto vā jñānī vā māṃ prapadyate
priyaḥ priyasya satataṃ jñāninastvasmi gocare
ananyadevatābhaktāḥ śraddhāvanto visaṃśayāḥ
vāsudevaḥ sarvamiti yajante māṃ mumukṣavaḥ
te brahmādhyātmakarmākhyaṃ sādhibhūtaṃ vidanti mām
sādhidaivādhiyajñaṃ ca dehavyuparameṣvapi
acyutenetyabhihite śakrasūnurabhāṣata
kimetadbrahma bhagavannadhiyajñaḥ kimucyate
iti pṛṣṭo hṛṣīkeśo babhāṣe śvetavāhanam
anaśvaraṃ parabrahma bhāvo 'dhyātmā tathātmanaḥ
niḥsaṅgo bhavakṛtkarma naśvareṣvadhibhūtatā
adhidaivo 'hamevātra hyadhiyajño 'pyahaṃ vibhuḥ
antakāle smaranto māṃ praviśantyeva bhāvitāḥ
paryante bhāvatulyā hi nṛṇāṃ janmāntarasthitiḥ
kaviṃ purāṇaṃ śāstāramaṇīyāṃsamaṇorapi
parastāttamaso nityaṃ ye smaranti raviprabham
bhrūmadhye vihitaprāṇā brahmarandhravibhedinaḥ
omityekākṣaraṃ brahma japanto yānti te param
brahmādibhirbhūtasargaścakravatparivartate
paraṃ māṃ pratipannāste na bhavanti bhave punaḥ
vairañce 'smin ahorātre bhavanti na bhavanti ca
bhūtānyekastu bhagavānavyakto na vinaśyati
tejomayamahaḥ śuklo mokṣāyaivottarāyaṇam
rājaguhyamidaṃ cānyatpavitraṃ śṛṇu phalguṇa
aśraddadhāno nāpnoti māṃ saṃsāravaśīkṛtaḥ
sarvakartari bhūtāni mayi santi na teṣvaham
lokāḥ sthitā na sthitāśca mayi vyomnīva vāyavaḥ
adhiṣṭhitaiṣā prakṛtirmayā sūte carācaram
asaktaṃ māṃ na jānanti malināmoghadarśinaḥ
sarvaṃ sarvagataṃ yajñaṃ vedyaṃ bījaṃ bhavābhavam
vidanti māṃ sukṛtinaḥ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam
trayīdharmajuṣaḥ svargabhogalābhakṣayākulāḥ
na prāpnuvanti māṃ śuṣkakriyāpāśavaśīkṛtāḥ
madekaśaraṇā nityaṃ kṛtino 'nanyayājinaḥ
apyanyayonisambhūtāḥ svayamāyānti yatpadam
bhūyo 'pi me śṛṇu sakhe prītyā yatpratibodhyase
na tattvenāmaragaṇā munayo vā vidanti mām
carācare 'sminpravaraṃ yadyatpaśyasi bhūtimat
tadahaṃ sarvabhūtātmā na hi kiṃcinmayā vinā
ahaṃ viṣṇurahaṃ sūryaścandro 'haṃ maghavānaham
śaṃkaro 'haṃ dhaneśaśca vahniḥ suragurustathā
akṣaro 'hamahaṃ kālo jayo 'haṃ bhūtirapyaham
śrutvaitadavadatpārtho jāne tvāṃ sarvamacyuta
kiṃtu viśvamayaṃ rūpaṃ draṣṭumicchāmi te vibho
ityuktaḥ pāṇḍuputreṇa bhagavānkaiṭabhāntakaḥ
viśvāviṣkārakalayā viśvarūpamadarśayat
tasyānantaśironetrasahasrabhujaśālinaḥ
dehe jagannivāsasya līnaṃ viśvamadṛśyata
atisūryāgnimahasā tejasā pūritāmbaram
dṛṣṭvā pulakitaḥ pārthastamuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ
paśyāmyudagragīrvāṇagrāmavyāptoruvigraham
tvāṃ yena pūritaṃ sarvam anavacchinnavarṣmaṇā
brahmarudramarudvahnimunīndrabhujagākulam
draṣṭuṃ tadeva paryantarahitaṃ notsahe vapuḥ
bhīṣmadroṇamukhānvīrānpraviṣṭānvadanāni te
daṃṣṭrotkaṭāni paśyāmi kālasyeva yugakṣaye
ko bhavānsarvasaṃhāraraudreṇa vapuṣāmunā
akāṇḍe dagdhumakhilānsvayaṃ lokānsamudyataḥ
ityuktavati kaunteye jagāda madhusūdanaḥ
ahaṃ jagatkṣayotkṣepadīkṣitaḥ kṣitipāntakaḥ
kurusenāgragānvīrānpūrvaṃ vinihatānmayā
hatvā yaśaḥśriyā juṣṭam avāpnuhi kulocitam
tacchrutvā kāliyārātervacaḥ pārthaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
uvāca kampitamanāḥ praṇato gadgadasvanaḥ
kīrtyā jaganti hṛṣyanti stutayā siddhacāraṇaiḥ
dīptyā dravanti rakṣāṃsi sthāne tava janārdana
naumi tvāṃ jagadāvāsaṃ viśvarūpamadhokṣajam
anantaṃ śāśvataṃ dhāma sarvātmānaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
kṣamyatāṃ tatsuhṛditi svayaṃ yatpraṇatapriyaḥ
ukto 'si kṛṣṇa govinda yādaveti purā mayā
ugraṃ tadevaṃ bhagavandṛṣṭvā rūpamahaṃ mahat
cakrārūḍhamivāśeṣaṃ paśyāmi nikhilaṃ jagat
prasīda darśaya vibho vapuḥ saumyaṃ tadeva me
śāntiṃ me yāti sahasā nānyathā vyathitaṃ manaḥ
iti prasāditaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ praṇatena kirīṭinā
adarśayannijaṃ rūpaṃ tadevātha caturbhujam
devā api na paśyanti mamedaṃ sarvagaṃ vapuḥ
ityuktvāśvāsayāmāsa kaunteyaṃ kamalādhavaḥ
athārjuno 'vadatkṛṣṇaṃ ye bhaktāstvāmupāsate
avyaktamakṣaraṃ ye ca teṣāṃ ke 'dhikayoginaḥ
pārtheneti hariḥ pṛṣṭo vihitānugraho 'vadat
madbhaktāḥ śraddhayopetāḥ sarvathā yogino 'dhikāḥ
kleśenaiva tu matprāptiravyaktākṣarasevanāt
sūkṣmasthūlagatirduḥkhaṃ tattvajñairapyavāpyate
madbhaktāstvacirādeva prāpnuvanti paraṃ padam
atastvaṃ manmanā nityam ananyanirato bhava
vaśe yadi na te cittam abhyāsena gṛhāṇa tat
tatrāpyaśakto matkarmā satataṃ śreyase bhava
athavā phalasaṃnyāsaṃ karmaṇāṃ kuru matparaḥ
jñānaṃ hi paramābhyāsājjñānāddhyānamihottamam
dhyānācca phalasaṃnyāsastataḥ śāntirviśiṣyate
adveṣṭā karuṇāsindhuḥ sukhaduḥkhasamaḥ śamī
udāsīnaḥ śucirdakṣaḥ kṣamī bhaktaḥ priyo mama
śarīraṃ kṣetramityāhuḥ kṣetrajñaṃ māṃ vidurbudhāḥ
kṣetraṃ tatsavikāraṃ tu māyā bhūtādi ca sthitam
śāntānāṃ dṛṣṭadoṣāṇāṃ jñānināṃ na vimohanam
mānadambhamadakrodhatyāgo guruniṣevaṇam
asaktir naśvare nityaṃ jñānam ajñānamanyathā
jñeyaṃ tu manmayaṃ brahma śuddhaṃ sadasatoḥ param
sarvataḥ pāṇivadanaṃ sarvākāramanāmayam
prakṛtiḥ puruṣaśceti kṣetrakṣetrajñasaṃgamaḥ
prakṛtiḥ karaṇe heturbhoktā tu puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ
ekasthānaṃ pṛthagbhāvaṃ bhūtānāṃ yo 'nupaśyati
tatsaṃgamācca vistāraṃ sa yāti brahma śāśvatam
paramātmā guṇātīto nityatvādayamavyayaḥ
bhautike 'pi sthitaḥ kāye sarvavyāpī na lipyate
sarvajñānamidaṃ bhūyaḥ śrūyatāṃ surasevitam
yadyogo brahmagarbhe 'sminsambhavanmūrtisaṃbhavaḥ
sattvādayastadudbhūtā vibhāntyete guṇāstrayaḥ
vaicitryādaniśaṃ yeṣāṃ saṃsaranti śarīriṇaḥ
sattvaṃ prakāśakaṃ jñeyaṃ yadutthaiḥ stambhakaṃ rajaḥ
tamo hyāvaraṇaṃ mohapramādādyasya saṃbhavaḥ
satataṃ saṃkareṇaiṣāṃ nyūnādhikyavibhedataḥ
guṇadoṣāśca dṛśyante te te kila śarīriṇām
madbhaktāḥ śāntamanaso jīvanmuktidaśāṃ śritāḥ
guṇairetaiḥ parityaktā bhajante sukhamakṣayam
ūrdhvamūlaṃ bhavāśvattham ābrahmasadanoditam
lokāntarānekaśākhaṃ vicitraviṣayāṅkuram
guṇakarmaprabuddhānāṃ śubhāśubhaphalodayam
svabhāvabhūmāvavṛtaṃ jānīte yaḥ sa vedavit
tamasaṅgakuṭhāreṇa chittvā yānti padaṃ mama
nirastamohaṃ vaimalyādatisūryendupāvakam
yadaṃśo jīvaloke 'smiñjīvaścarati sarvagaḥ
vāyurgandhamivādāya yo yātīndriyavāsanāḥ
tadvidhaṃ guṇayuktānāṃ sarvāvasthāsu nirguṇam
paśyanti jñāninaḥ sarvajagatāṃ jīvanaṃ param
bhūtasargam ivāgatya akṣaro 'haṃ sanātanaḥ
manmayā dhṛtimanto māṃ bhajante puruṣottamam
abhīḥ sattvaṃ śucirjñānaṃ damo dānaṃ tapaḥ kratuḥ
ahiṃsāyā guṇāścānye jāyante divyasaṃpadām
dambhamānamadakrodhapāruṣyājñānacāpalaiḥ
āsurī sūcyate saṃpanmohaśokavivardhinī
yukto 'pi satataṃ divyasaṃpadā mā śucaḥ sakhe
āsuraṃ bhāvamāpannā bhajante yonimāsurīm
sattvādibhirguṇairbaddho jñāyate ceṣṭitairjanaḥ
manobhojanamācāro guṇatulyo hi dehinām
ākarṇyaitadathovāca phalgunaḥ punaracyutam
saṃnyāsatyāgayos tattvaṃ jñātumicchāmyahaṃ vibho
ukte pāṇḍusuteneti bhagavānabhyabhāṣata
kāmyakarmaphalatyāgaṃ saṃnyāsaṃ sampracakṣate
sarvakarmaphalatyāgas tyāga ityabhidhīyate
matkarma na parityājyaṃ tyājyaṃ tu vidhigarhitam
nityakarmaparityāgo mohāttāmasa ucyate
kleśaduḥkhabhayāttyāgo rājaso niṣphalaḥ smṛtaḥ
kurvatāmapyasaktānāṃ tyāgaḥ sattvocito mataḥ
karma kartā ca buddhiśca trividhā guṇabhedataḥ
dhṛtiḥ sukhaṃ ca traiguṇyāttrividhaṃ dehināṃ matam
yathoktasevī niḥsaṅgaḥ kuru karma nijaṃ sakhe
madbhakto matstutiparaḥ paraṃ padamavāpsyasi
idaṃ bhaktāya te jñānamupadiṣṭaṃ mayā svayam
yaḥ śroṣyati sa saṃsāraduḥkhānyatitariṣyati
kaccinmoho vinaṣṭaste kaccidetacchrutaṃ tvayā
keśaveneti kathite babhāṣe śakranandanaḥ
bhagavanvītamoho 'haṃ kariṣye tava śāsanam
uktveti vīro gāṇḍīvamācakarṣa raṇotsukaḥ
athodatiṣṭhadgambhīrajaladadhvānamantharaḥ
yuyutsuṃ pārthamālokya sainyānāṃ harṣaniḥsvanaḥ
pūrvaṃ tataḥ subhaṭakaṅkaṭapātikhaḍgaṭāṅkāranādamukhareṣu baleṣu rājñām
dharmātmajaḥ kavacacāpaśarānvimucya devavratābhimukhamutsukadhīḥ sasarpa
dhigdhiṅnṛpaṃ kṛpaṇaceṣṭa manuṣyasaṃjñaṃ bhīruṃ yudhiṣṭhiramalīkakṛtābhidhānam
yācñā kṛtāñjalirupaiti parānyadeṣa śūrāstadiṅgitajaḍāḥ pṛthagityavocan
so 'pyacchakīrtiratha bhīṣmamukhānupetya prahvaḥ śarīrapaṇasaṃśritadhārtarāṣṭrān
tatpādalagnamukuṭaḥ prakaṭaṃ praṇamya lebhe tadāśiṣamaśeṣamahīpajaitrīm
abhyāhate ca raṇaraṅgamṛdaṅgatūrye pārthānguṇaikarasiko guṇavānyuyutsuḥ
abhyāyayau tava sutaḥ svakurūnnirasya dhāvanti tulyaguṇameva nṛṇāṃ manāṃsi
asminmahākṣayamukhe karavālapaṭṭasaṃrakṣitapratimukhe raṇaraṅganāṭye
vyākīrṇakīrtikusumāñjalir arjunāgre nāndīmivāpaṭhadamandadhanurninādaiḥ
atrāntare nṛpaticakrakirīṭakoṭisaṃpātajātabahuśākulavisphuliṅga
jaitrī triśūlakaraśiṣyamunerudagrā gāṅgeyaśātaviśikhāvalir ullalāsa
saṃtrāsasaṃkucitaniścalakarṇatāladikkuñjarākalitakampitasarvalokam
kṣubhyatkṣayāmbudharabhairavabhīmanādaṃ bhīmaṃ niśamya bhayamāvirabhūdbhaṭānām
atha bhīmaṃ samabhyāyāt svayaṃ rājā suyodhanaḥ
bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito vīrairdhunāno vipulaṃ dhanuḥ
tataḥ pravṛtte saṃgrāme durlakṣye śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
svayaṃ śāntanavaḥ śrīmānabhyadhāvaddhanaṃjayam
sātyakiṃ kṛtavarmā ca hyabhimanyuṃ bṛhadbalaḥ
duḥśāsano 'pi nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca durmukhaḥ
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ tathā śalya ācāryo drupadātmajam
somadattaśca vairāṭiṃ bāhlikaścedibhūpatim
rakṣasāṃ pravaraṃ vīraṃ ghaṭotkacam alumbusaḥ
śikhaṇḍinaṃ droṇasuto matsyaṃ prāgjyotiṣeśvaraḥ
kṛpaḥ kekayabhūpālaṃ drupadaṃ ca jayadrathaḥ
sutasomaṃ vikarṇaśca bhīmasenasutaṃ balī
cekitānaḥ vikarṇaśca prativindhyaṃ ca saubalaḥ
irāvataśca vikrāntaṃ śatāyuḥ phalguṇātmajam
vindānuvindāvāvantyau kuntibhojaṃ yaśasvinam
kauravo vīrabāhuśca virāṭasutamuttaram
anye ca vīrā rājāno rājasiṃhāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
utsāhasattvasampannāḥ sasainyāḥ yamupādravan
teṣāṃ kaṅkaṇaratnāṃśupaṭalāḥ karanirgatāḥ
hemapuṅkhāḥ śarāścakrurvahnivyāptaṃ digantaram
athoddhatena rajasā gajavājirathākulam
vīrāṇāṃ tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ nirmaryādamavartata
tataḥ śirobhirvīrāṇāṃ patitotphullitair muhuḥ
amandakandukakrīḍā babhūveva raṇaśriyaḥ
tataḥ pāṇḍavasainyeṣu bhīṣmacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
vidāriteṣu bahuśaḥ samuttasthau mahāravaḥ
athābhimanyurabhyetya śatamanyusutātmajaḥ
bhīṣmamabhyādravadvīro miṣatāṃ sarvabhūbhujām
kṛtavarmaprabhṛtibhiḥ sahitaṃ bhīṣmamojasā
ayodhayatsa viśikhairdhvajamasya cakarta ca
hematāle nipatite saṃrabdho 'tha pitāmahaḥ
divyāsravarṣī sāvegaṃ saubhadraṃ samupādravat
tato vṛkodaramukhā vinadanto mahārathāḥ
sānugaṃ śantanusutaṃ samantātparyavārayan
bhīṣmo 'pi sātyakiṃ viddhvā dhvajaṃ pavanajanmanaḥ
unmamātha śarāgreṇa haimaṃ kesariṇaṃ rathāt
atrāntare giriprāṃśumāruhya madakuñjaram
ayodhayanmadrarājaṃ hṛṣṭo vairāṭiruttaraḥ
sa kuñjarendraḥ śalyasya pādena caturo hayān
jaghānākṛṣya hastena garjañjaladaniḥsvanaḥ
tato madrādhipaḥ kruddhaḥ śaktiṃ śaktimatāṃ varaḥ
pradīptāṃ prāhiṇodvegāduttarāyeṣuvarṣiṇe
sa tayā bhinnahṛdayaḥ papāta galitāyudhaḥ
karṇikāra iva bhraṣṭaḥ karīndrācalaśekharāt
uttaraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā śaṅkhastasyānujaḥ krudhā
cakāra śalyamabhyetya śarairjaṭilavigraham
tasya śalyo 'tha gadayā vidārya dalaśo ratham
unnanādābhavanyena diśaḥ śakalitā iva
śaṅkho hatāśvaḥ sahasā phalguṇasya rathaṃ yayau
bhīṣmo 'tha pāṇḍavacamūṃ vyagāhata nṛpāntakaḥ
matsyakekayapāñcālacedisenāsu sarvaśaḥ
bhīṣmabāṇavibhinnāsu sūryo 'staśikharaṃ yayau
tato nivṛtte saṃgrāme śibirāṇi nareśvarāḥ
bhejire pratiśaṃsanto vipulaṃ bhīṣmavikramam
dinānte dīrṇapṛtanaḥ śokārto dharmanandanaḥ
saṃhāraṃ nijasainyānāṃ pradadhyau bhīṣmavikramam
sa rājamadhye govindamuvāca karuṇākulaḥ
kṣīyamāṇasya samare satyaṃ śreyastapo mama
alaṃ yuddhena me kṛṣṇa pṛthivīkṣayakāriṇā
ko mucyeta raṇe prāpya bhīṣmaṃ bhīṣmaparākramam
iti bruvāṇaṃ rājānamuvāca madhusūdanaḥ
dhruvaste vijayo rājanyasya yoddhā dhanaṃjayaḥ
sātyakirdrupadaḥ śaibyaḥ śikhaṇḍī pañca kekayāḥ
saubhadraśca raṇe kruddho hanyādeva gaṇānapi
ukte janārdaneneti tīvraṃ bhīṣmaparākramam
mithaḥ kathayatāṃ teṣāṃ sā jagāma vibhāvarī
athodite sahasrāṃśau vihite pāṇḍunandanaiḥ
kruñcavyūhe mahotsāhair vyūhamanye 'pi cakrire
tataḥ pravṛtte samare tīvre bhīrubhayaṃkare
hṛdayākampane nājñāṃ tālaketuradṛśyata
gambhīradhīrasaṃrambho varjayansa pṛthagjanam
cakarta bhūbhujāmeva śirāṃsi laghuvikramaḥ
bhīṣmeṇālolite vyūhe vātoddhūta ivārṇave
tamabhyadhāvatsaṃrabdhaḥ śvetāśvo 'cyutasārathiḥ
tamāpatantaṃ viśikhairbhīṣmaḥ kṣipramapūrayat
droṇaduryodhanamukhāḥ sarve cānye mahārathāḥ
pārtho 'pi sāyakaiścakre samantātkuruvāhinīm
tatpakṣapavanasphārairdīrṇāmiva sahasradhā
duryodhanaprerito 'tha svayaṃ śantanunandanaḥ
nindannijaṃ kṣatradharmam abhyadhāvad dhanaṃjayam
nirviśeṣaṃ tayostatra suciraṃ yudhyamānayoḥ
niruddhāḥ śarajālena nādṛśyanta diśo daśa
na dadarśa tayoḥ kaścidantaraṃ kṣipatoḥ śarān
dhārāsāraprabalayornadatoriva meghayoḥ
tato droṇamukhā vīrā dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamaiḥ
ayudhyantābhavanyena surāḥ pulakitā divi
bhīmasenaḥ kaliṅgānāṃ praviśyātha varūthinīm
pātayankuñjarāṃścakre niḥsaṃcārāṃ vasuṃdharām
bhīmanirbhinnamattebhakumbhodbhūtāsṛgambhasām
pravāhairyayurākaṇṭhaṃ turaṅgāḥ kṛcchragāminaḥ
nihatya kuñjarānīkaṃ kaliṅgānāṃ prahāriṇām
ketumantaṃ narapatiṃ jaghāna sapadānugam
niḥśeṣitakaliṅgasya bhīmasenasya nādataḥ
ghanagambhīranādena pṛthivī samakampata
tato bhīṣmaḥ samabhyetya dṛṣṭvā dīrṇāmanīkinīm
vidhāya virathaṃ bhīmaṃ śaineyāśvānapothayat
duryodhanasutaṃ vīraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ śauryalakṣaṇam
abhimanyuḥ śitairbāṇaiḥ kṣiprahastamapothayat
gocare patitaṃ putraṃ saubhadrasya pramāthinaḥ
dṛṣṭvā duryodhano rājā sānugaḥ svayamādravat
kuruvīraiḥ parivṛtaṃ vilokya sutamarjunaḥ
maṇḍalīkṛtagāṇḍīvastūrṇaṃ pratyudyayau parān
lāghavādabhitastasya sāyakāścitrayodhinaḥ
jahnuḥ śirāṃsi śūrāṇāṃ phalānīva mahīruhām
ākhaṇḍalabhuvā caṇḍagāṇḍīvapreritaiḥ śaraiḥ
vidāriteṣvanīkeṣu vidhvastarathasādiṣu
rudhireṇeva gagane saṃdhyārāgeṇa pūrite
avahāraṃ raṇe cakre vāsarānte pitāmahaḥ
anyedyurgāruḍaṃ vyūhaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmeṇa kalpitam
ardhacandraṃ prativyūhaṃ cakrire pāṇḍunandanāḥ
tataḥ pravṛtte samare bhīrūṇāṃ dhṛtikhaṇḍane
ārūḍheva mahīvyoma rajasā samalakṣyata
asṛkpravāhaiḥ sahasā praśānte reṇumaṇḍale
sughoraḥ saṃprahāro 'bhūnnṛpāṇāṃ tridaśekṣitaḥ
bhīṣmadroṇamukhairvīraiḥ phalguṇapramukhā raṇe
saṃsaktāḥ samadṛśyanta pūrvadevairivāmarāḥ
bāṇajālena mahatā saṃhatānāṃ samantataḥ
arjunena niruddhāsu ripūṇāṃ śastravṛṣṭiṣu
akampitau kuruvyūhe bhīmasenaghaṭotkacau
praviśya cakraturvīrau vyākulāṃ paravāhinīm
tāvabhyadhāvatsaṃrambhādamarṣī dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ
kurvanrājasamājena mauliratnāruṇā diśaḥ
haiḍambabāṇanihatā vīrāstasya padānugāḥ
mahāvātasamākrāntā drumā iva cakampire
duryodhanapreritānāṃ śarāṇāṃ dīptatejasām
vṛṣṭimabhyudgatāṃ ghorāṃ cichedāśu vṛkodaraḥ
bhīmotsṛṣṭena pṛthunā pṛṣatkenātha kauravaḥ
hṛdi viddho nimagnena mumoha bhṛśavihvalaḥ
tasminsārathinā nīte rathenākulaketunā
dudrāva sainyaṃ tatsarvaṃ paśyatordroṇabhīṣmayoḥ
mahārathairvārite 'pi kīrṇe tasminbalārṇave
pratyudyayau samāśvasya tūrṇaṃ rājā suyodhanaḥ
pārthasātyakisaubhadraiḥ sa dṛṣṭvā bahuśaścamūm
vidrāvitāṃ samabhyetya pitāmahamabhāṣata
dāritaṃ paśya me sainyaṃ labdhalakṣairarātibhiḥ
pāṇḍuputreṣu kṛpayā tvayi mādhyasthyamāśrite
alaṃ droṇasahāyasya paristhātuṃ purastava
madabhāgyavaśānna syādyadi pārtheṣu vaḥ kṛpā
etatsuyodhanenoktaṃ śrutvā surasaritsutaḥ
īṣatsmitasudhādhautakapolaphalako 'vadat
ukto 'si bahuśo rājannajeyāḥ pāṇḍavā iti
yattu śakyaṃ mayā kiṃcidvṛddhenādya karomi kim
ityuktvā cāpamākṛṣya tālamātraṃ mahābhujaḥ
mandāyamāne divase samamabhyudyayau parān
tato bhīṣmarathodīrṇaiḥ śaraiḥ sūryakaraprabhaiḥ
vidāritānyanekāni tamāṃsīva kṣayaṃ yayuḥ
tomareṣvātapatreṣu śarīreṣu ca bhūbhujām
petuḥ punarabhāvāya bhīṣmanāmāṅkitāḥ śarāḥ
adṛṣṭapuṅkhavadanairghanaśreṇīkṛtairmuhuḥ
tatsāyakair adṛśyābhūt pāṇḍavānām anīkinī
taṃ yudhyamānaṃ dīptāstraṃ varjayanto 'pi saṃgare
dikṣu bhīṣmasahasrāṇi dadṛśuḥ sarvapārthivāḥ
vrajatsu rājacakreṣu bhīṣmānalapataṅgatām
ekenaikena bāṇena bhinneṣu triṣu dantiṣu
yāte sahasradhā sainye pāṇḍavānāṃ tarasvinām
anayatphalguṇarathaṃ gāṅgeyāntikamacyutaḥ
tato 'bhavadbhīṣmaśarairbhāsvaraiḥ savyasācinaḥ
kṣaṇaṃ pañcānanasyeva cārukāñcanapañjaraḥ
niruddhaśarasaṃcāro yatnena śatamanyujaḥ
vicitrairvicaranmārgairyuyudhe kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
tasyātimānuṣaṃ dhairyamāsthitasya pitāmahaḥ
sādhu putreti saṃhṛṣṭaḥ parākramamapūjayat
tatkaṅkapattrinirbhinnau kṛṣṇāvekarathe sthitau
raktāśokāvivotphullau babhatuḥ kṣatajokṣitau
tato nirantarairbāṇairbhīṣmakārmukanirgataiḥ
ākrāntabhuvanābhogairnādṛśyanta diśo daśa
bhīṣme pṛthuśarajvāle kālānala ivodyate
dudrāva pāṇḍavacamūḥ paścādabhisṛtā paraiḥ
bhagneṣu bhaṭamukhyeṣu babhāṣe kaiṭabhāntakaḥ
kva nu mānadhanā yūyamapārayaśaso raṇe
parityajya kulācāraṃ yātāḥ kātaratāmimām
ityuktvā tānsamālokya vidrutāneva keśavaḥ
uvāca sātyakiṃ vīraṃ yudhyamānaṃ prayatnataḥ
tiṣṭhantu yāntu vā sarve sātyake pṛtanāgragāḥ
eṣa svayaṃ nihanmyadya sānugaṃ śantanoḥ sutam
ityuktvā caṇḍamārtaṇḍamaṇḍalāgraṃ sudarśanam
svayamudyamya kaṃsāriḥ syandanāgrādavātarat
kruddhasya tasya kalpāntakarālānalarociṣaḥ
na rūpaṃ sehire draṣṭuṃ surā api divi sthitāḥ
saṃrambhodbhrāntadordaṇḍavilasatpītavāsasā
śobhāṃ bheje sa nīlādreḥ sarpatsaṃdhyābhraśālinaḥ
tamantakamivāyāntaṃ jagatsaṃhāradīkṣitam
dhīraḥ śāntanavo dṛṣṭvā dhunāno dhanurabhyadhāt
ehyehi bhagavanviṣṇo jiṣṇo tridaśavidviṣām
cakreṇa me śiraśchinddhi bhavakleśakṛśānunā
bhavatā nābhijāmbhojasamuddhūtasvayaṃbhuvā
hato jagannivāsena dhanyatāṃ yātvayaṃ janaḥ
siddhasindhusuteneti bhāṣite natamaulinā
avaruhya rathāttūrṇam arjunaḥ kṛṣṇamanvagāt
sa niṣpīḍya balātpādau purastātkāliyadviṣaḥ
uvāca saṃhara vibho kopaṃ viśvakṣayocitam
kṣapayāmi ripūnsarvānyudhi satyena te śape
iti prasādya taṃ pārtho rathamāropayatpunaḥ
tato gāṇḍīvaghoṣeṇa pāñcajanyaraveṇa ca
cakrāte rājacakrāṇāṃ kṛṣṇau kṛṣṇāmbudabhramam
tato nirvivarairbāṇaiḥ śalyabhūriśravaḥśalāḥ
avākiranbhīṣmamukhāḥ phalguṇaṃ śastravṛṣṭibhiḥ
tāmāyudhamahāvṛṣṭiṃ chittvā sapadi pāṇḍavaḥ
māhendramastraṃ vidadhe sarvalokakṣayakṣamam
tasmin udīrṇe sahasā mahāstre dīptatejasi
caṇḍavātavikīrṇeva cakampe kuruvāhinī
vadhyamāneṣu sainyeṣu kṣipraṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
naranāgāśvadehotthā sasarpa rudhirāpagā
chattrācchaphenapaṭalāṃ calaccāmarasārasām
keśaśevālaśabalāṃ piśācāstāṃ siṣevire
ghore nṛpakṣaye tasminvartamāne raṇotsave
saṃdhyayā dikṣu jātāsu śoṇitena bhṛtāsviva
yāte 'staṃ caṇḍakiraṇe pratyagrarudhiratviṣi
māṃsapiṇḍa iva graste ghoreṇa dhvāntarakṣasā
vidhvastacāpakavacā viprakīrṇarathadhvajāḥ
avahāramakurvanta pāṇḍavāḥ śastravikṣatāḥ
punaḥ prabhāte saṃrabdhā niryayuḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ
vinadanto mahotsāhā vyāḍavyūhāgravartinaḥ
atha pravṛtte samare pṛthivīkṣayaśaṃsini
saubhadrapramukhā vīrānbhīṣmamukhyānayodhayan
tataḥ śaraśatāsārasampūritadigantaraḥ
mahārathān atītyānyān bhīṣmo 'rjunamupādravat
nirviśeṣaṃ tayoḥ kṣipraṃ vīrayor yudhyamānayoḥ
eko droṇimukhānvīrānabhimanyurayodhayat
chinnavarmadhvajarathānsa vidhāya mahārathān
śiraḥprakaramucchinnaṃ rājñāṃ kṣipramapātayat
droṇaprabhṛtibhiḥ sarvairdṛṣṭvā saubhadramāvṛtam
dhṛṣṭadyumnaścamūnāthaścakartābhyetya kauravān
sa hatvā cāmaraṃ śūraḥ pauravyatanayaṃ nṛpam
śiraḥ saṃyamaneḥ kāyājjahārākulakuṇḍalam
atrāntare gajānīkairvipulaiśca gajādhipaḥ
bhīmaduryodhanādiṣṭo gadāpāṇiḥ samādravat
bhīmaseno 'tha rabhasādavaruhya rathādgajān
garjannurugadāghātairjaghāna ghanavikramaḥ
gadāprahārābhihatairvajrabhinnairivācalaiḥ
patadbhirmattamātaṅgaiścakampe cakiteva bhūḥ
nihate kuñjarānīke bhīmena bhayadāyinā
tamabhyadhāvansaṃkruddhāḥ sarve duryodhanādayaḥ
suyodhanaśarāghātamūrchito 'tha vṛkodaraḥ
samāśvāsya parānīkaṃ rathena kupito 'viśat
viśvasaṃhārasaṃkruddhaṃ taṃ kṛtāntamivotthitam
prāpyānujāḥ kurupateścaturdaśa yayuḥ kṣayam
senāpatiṃ suṣeṇaṃ ca jayasaṃdhaṃ sulocanam
bhīmamugraṃ bhīmarathaṃ bhīmabāhumalolupam
samaṃ vivitsuṃ kaṭakaṃ durmukhaṃ duṣpradarśanam
hatvaināmakarotsenāṃ kauravāṇāṃ sahasradhā
tamabhyadhāvanmattena supratīkena dantinā
gambhīraghoraghoṣeṇa bhagadattaḥ sahānugaiḥ
gajodayācalaraveḥ śaraistīkṣṇairivāṃśubhiḥ
pratāpadhāmnastasyārātsa ca kopārivāhinī
tatsāyakena viddho 'tha hṛdi marmāvabhedinā
dhvajayaṣṭiṃ samālambya tasthau bhīmo 'timūrchitaḥ
tato ghaṭotkacaḥ kruddho dṛṣṭvā janakamākulam
bhagadattamabhidrutya ghorāṃ māyāṃ samādade
airāvaṇagataḥ so 'tha prabhinnairdigdvipaiḥ saha
apīḍayatsupratīkaṃ dīptābhiḥ śastravṛṣṭibhiḥ
tasya nirbhidyamānasya kuñjarendrasya garjataḥ
śabdena tasthurālīya sarve saṃkucitā gajāḥ
ghaṭotkacena saṃsaktaṃ dṛṣṭvā prāgjyotiṣeśvaram
saha droṇādibhirvīrairbhīṣmastaṃ deśamādravat
ghaṭotkacaṃ kālarūpaṃ nadantaṃ vīkṣya bhairavam
saṃdhyāyāṃ durjayaṃ matvā bhīṣmastaṃ bhīmavikramam
avahāraṃ susainyānāṃ vidadhe dhīmatāṃ varaḥ
yenābhavankālavaktrānniṣkrāntā iva kauravāḥ
tato niśāyāmabhyetya kururājaḥ pitāmaham
papraccha pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ duḥkhito jayakāraṇam
tamabravīcchāntanavo rājannukto 'si sarvadā
devena viṣṇunā guptā na jeyāḥ pāṇḍavā iti
purā bhūbhāraśāntyarthaṃ svayaṃbhūrmunisaṃsadi
prādurbhūtaṃ svayaṃ viṣṇuṃ tuṣṭāva sahasāṃ nidhim
jaya viśveśa viśvātmanviśvaksena sudhānidhe
amandaciddhanānanda saṃvitsamarasadyute
namastubhyaṃ jagatsargasthitisaṃhārakāriṇe
trivikramāya mahate triguṇāya trimūrtaye
namaḥ pracaṇḍacakrāgraprabhābhāsurabāhave
daityāndhakārasaṃhārakāriṇe mohadāriṇe
avatīrṇā bhuvaṃ nātha dānavā ye hatāstvayā
teṣāṃ vadhāya dṛptānāṃ mānuṣīṃ tanumāviśa
iti stutāḥ padmabhuvā devo nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
nareṇa sākaṃ bhūbhāraśāntyai kṣitimavātarat
sa eṣa kṛṣṇo bhagavāñjāto yādavanandanaḥ
naraśca vijayo dhīraḥ pravaraḥ sarvadhanvinām
devau kṛṣṇārjunāvetau na jeyau tridaśairapi
iti jñātvā śamaḥ putra kriyatāṃ pāṇḍunandanaiḥ
atha prabhāte makaraśyenavyūhāgravartinaḥ
bhīṣmabhīmamukhā yuddhaṃ cakrire pāṇḍunandanāḥ
hatānāṃ hanyamānānāṃ ghnatāṃ ca samare mithaḥ
patatāṃ tatra vīrāṇāṃ svanastumulo 'bhavat
bhīmaphalguṇasaubhadramatsyasātyakipārṣataiḥ
bhīṣmamukhyaiśca te sene bhinne saṃśayamāpatuḥ
kabandhatāṇḍavaścaṇḍe mattavetālasaṃkule
tasmin āyodhane ghore bhūtānāmutsavo 'bhavat
dhanvināṃ śarajālena divamutpatatāṃ muhuḥ
ravau saṃchādite rājñāṃ vyartho 'bhūcchastrasaṃgrahaḥ
vīreṇa bhūriśravasā saṃsaktaṃ vīkṣya sātyakim
abhyādravan dhanvinastaṃ deśaṃ sātyakisūnavaḥ
teṣāmāpatatāṃ pūrṇaṃ sṛjatāṃ śaradurdinam
bhūriśravāḥ śirāṃsy ārād uccakarta śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
hateṣu teṣu kupitaḥ pradīptāstro dhanaṃjayaḥ
cakāra kurusenānāṃ saṃhāraṃ harisārathiḥ
hate lakṣacaturbhāge bhūbhujāmanivartinām
gāṇḍīvadhanvanā sainyaṃ vāsarānte nyavartata
punaḥ prabhāte saṃnaddhā niryayuḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ
alakṣyabhedāvyūhābhyāṃ krauñcena makareṇa ca
tataḥ pramathya sahasā bhīmaseno 'rivāhinīm
viveśa bhṛśasaṃkruddhaḥ samaṃ drupadasūnunā
tābhyāṃ vidārite vyūhe kupitāḥ kurunandanāḥ
vimukhaiḥ kuñjarānīkaistau tūrṇaṃ paryavārayan
bhīmasenagadāghātaniṣpiṣṭavapuṣāṃ raṇe
abhūdvyatikaro ghoraḥ patatāṃ gajayodhinām
yudhyamāneṣu sainyeṣu bhīmena bhujaśālinā
abhyādravatsānugastaṃ svayaṃ rājā suyodhanaḥ
chāditaṃ kauravairdṛṣṭvā bhīmaṃ viśikhavarṣibhiḥ
vimohaṃ vidadhe teṣāṃ mohanāstreṇa pārṣataḥ
droṇena svayamabhyetya jñānāstreṇa vināśite
mohanāstre kurupatiṃ bhīmastūrṇamupādravat
madāndha kvādhunā jīvanmayi jīvati yāsyasi
ityuktvā te śaraśatairvajravegairavākiran
bhīmacāpacyutairbāṇaiḥ so 'tha kṛttarathadhvajaḥ
hṛdi nirdārito bheje mūrchāṃ vyathitamānasaḥ
atrāntare bhīṣmaśarairhanyamāneṣu rājasu
ghoro babhūva saṃmardaḥ kṛtāntasamarotsavaḥ
draupadeyeṣu vīreṣu yudhyamāneṣu kauravaiḥ
avartata raṇo ghoro gajavājirathakṣayaḥ
athāvahāraṃ sainyānāṃ cakre śantanunandanaḥ
rājasevāvṛte sūrye yāte 'staṃ rudhirāruṇe
anyedyurmaṇḍalavyūhe bhīṣmeṇa vihite svayam
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sa durbhedyaṃ vajravyūhamakalpayat
tataḥ pravṛtte samare bhīṣaṇe bhīṣmapārthayoḥ
virāṭa ādravaddroṇaṃ gariṣṭhaṃ sarvadhanvinām
droṇastaṃ bāṇavarṣeṇa saṃchādya śaravarṣiṇam
unnanāda dhanadhvāno rathamasya jaghāna ca
sa hatāśvaṃ samutsṛjya rathaṃ putrasya saṃbhramāt
āruroha hatānīkaṃ śaṅkhasyārūḍhadhanvinaḥ
droṇo 'tha tau pitāputrau vilokyaikarathe sthitau
śaṅkhāya prāhiṇodghoraṃ mṛtyudaṇḍopamaṃ śaram
sa tena bhinnahṛdayaḥ papāta kṣatajokṣitaḥ
vātenonmathitaḥ śailādutphulla iva kiṃśukaḥ
tataḥ śikhaṇḍinaṃ droṇaḥ śarairviśikhavarṣiṇam
hatāśve sātyakirathaṃ samārūḍhe śikhaṇḍini
alambuso rākṣasendraḥ krūrakarmā tamādravat
māyayā yudhyamānaṃ taṃ garjantaṃ rākṣaseśvaram
cakāra vimukhaṃ kopādraudreṇāstreṇa sātyakiḥ
śaineyena jite tasmin irāvān arjunātmajaḥ
vindānuvindāvabhyāyājjambhārisamavikramaḥ
ghaṭotkacamathāyāntaṃ kṛtāntamiva bhairavam
avārayadgajendreṇa bhagadatto nṛpāgraṇīḥ
vīraṃ sa hatvā haiḍambaṃ pāṇḍavānāmanīkinīm
darpādviloḍayāmāsa gajendro nalinīmiva
mādrīsutau tataḥ śalyaṃ vidhāya virathaṃ śaraiḥ
cakraturvimukhaṃ saṃkhye rājacakrasya paśyataḥ
svayaṃ yudhiṣṭhiro rājā nṛpaṃ jitvā śrutāyudham
vigāhya kauravānīkaṃ vidadhe vimukhaṃ śaraiḥ
cekitānena vijite gautame dhanvināṃ gurau
bhīṣmaścakāra kadanaṃ rājñāmanyatra cārjunaḥ
yudhiṣṭhiragirā vīkṣya bhīṣmāya samabhidravat
śikhaṇḍinaṃ madrarājo divyairastrairavārayat
bhīṣmeṇa hanyamāneṣu bhūpāleṣvanivartiṣu
pārthena ca trigarteṣu jagāmāstaṃ divākaraḥ
tamobhirāvṛte loke raṇe raktāsavākule
pramattairiva vetālaiḥ śibirāṇi yayurnṛpāḥ
bhīṣmeṇa sāgaravyūhe prātarviracite punaḥ
śṛṅgāṭakaṃ mahāvyūhaṃ cakre drupadanandanaḥ
vidīrṇeṣviva sainyeṣu bhīṣmacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
babhūvābhimukhaḥ kopādeka eva vṛkodaraḥ
sa hatvā sārathiṃ bāṇaistūrṇaṃ śantanujanmanaḥ
droṇasya ca samudbhrāntapatākaṃ vidadhe ratham
labdhalakṣyastato bhīmaḥ sapta duryodhanānujān
jaghāna madasaṃrabdhānpañcānana iva dvipān
bahvāśinaṃ kuṇḍadhāraṃ viśālākṣaṃ sudurjayam
mahodaraṃ maṇḍitakaṃ sunābhaṃ ca nihatya tān
vidrāvya kauravacamūṃ nanādāsphālayandiśaḥ
kṣayāya sarvajagatāṃ devai rudra ivoditaḥ
irāvānatha vikrānto viveśa kuruvāhinīm
ulūpī nāgalalanā phalgunādyamajījanat
kāryaṃ samarasāhāyyaṃ svayamityarjunena saḥ
uktaḥ purā surapure tāṃ yuddhabhuvamāyayau
ratnakāñcanasaṃnāhaiḥ sa pātālaturaṅgamaiḥ
uhyamānaḥ śaraiścakre phaṇilokamivāparam
sa gatvā vipulānīkāngāndhārānhayayodhinaḥ
śakunestanayānsapta jaghāna ghanavikramān
tato duryodhanādiṣṭo māyāvī rākṣasādhipaḥ
alambusaḥ samabhyāyādirāvantaṃ raṇotkaṭaḥ
irāvānatha khaḍgena chittvā sapadi rakṣasaḥ
sa niṣaṅgaṃ dhanurdīptaṃ nanāda balināṃ varaḥ
tato māyāṃ samāśritya mahatīṃ mohanīṃ nṛṇām
yuyudhāte samāviśya tau nabho bhīmavikramau
irāvatā nijāstraughairhanyamānasya rakṣasaḥ
ghoraḥ samudabhūnnādaḥ sarvaprāṇibhayaṃkaraḥ
atha sāhāyyakaṃ cakrurbhujaṅgā bhujagībhuvaḥ
tadvamanto viṣaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ bhogānbhogabhṛtāṃ varāḥ
rākṣaso 'tha bhṛśaṃ kruddho rūpamāsthāya gāruḍam
bhakṣayitvākhilānsarpānbhīmaṃ svaṃ vapurādade
māyāvimohitasyātha khaḍgenārādirāvataḥ
jahāra rākṣasaṃ kāyācchirastalakuṇḍalam
hate dhanaṃjayasute haiḍambaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
rurāva yena vasudhā cacāla sakulācalā
tamabhidrutamālokya rājā duryodhanaḥ svayam
saha sarvair nijānīkair mahāmāyam ayodhayat
vidyujjihvaṃ vegavantaṃ mahāraudraṃ pramāthinam
haiḍimbānucarānghorānsa jaghāna niśācarān
śaktiṃ ghaṭotkacenātha preritāṃ kurubhūbhuje
mahāgajena jagrāha vaṅgānāmadhipaḥ puraḥ
nāge nipatite tasminrakṣite ca suyodhane
saṃhāraṃ purusainyānāṃ cakāra piśitāśanaḥ
bhagadatto 'tha vidrāvya pāṇḍavānāmanīkinīm
supratīkena nāgena ghaṭotkacamayodhayat
tanayaṃ nihataṃ śrutvā kupitaḥ śatamanyujaḥ
śirobhirbhūmipālānāṃ durgamāṃ vasudhāṃ vyadhāt
bhīmo 'pi krodhasaṃtapto bhrātuḥ putre nipātite
suyodhanānujānvīrānprāhiṇodyamamandiram
anādhṛṣṭiṃ kuṇḍalinaṃ kuṇḍabhediṃ sulocanam
virāṭaṃ dīrghabāhuṃ ca subāhuṃ kanakadhvajam
hatvaitānkauravānīkaṃ kabandhaśatasaṃkulam
vidadhe mattavetālanandane dinasaṃkṣaye
visrastacāpakavace bhagnasyandanakuñjare
raṇe 'vahāraṃ sainyānāṃ tataścakrurmahārathāḥ
tato niśāyāmanujaiḥ saha rājā suyodhanaḥ
karṇam ānāyya pārthānāṃ parābhavamacintayat
vaikartanastamavadatkriyatāṃ madvacaḥ sakhe
śastraṃ nyāsaya gāṅgeyamahaṃ jeṣyāmi pāṇḍavān
eṣa vṛddho nirīhaśca sapakṣaśca dhanaṃjaye
tvayā nyasto 'tibhāro 'smin avicāryaiva kevalam
etadākarṇya karṇoktaṃ harṣātkarmaśatairiva
utthāya bhīṣmaśibiraṃ pratasthe bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
maṇidīpasahasrāṃśupiṅgīkṛtadigantaraḥ
naktaṃ dīptauṣadhivanaḥ sakulādririvābabhau
ratnakuṇḍalakeyūrakirīṭadyutinirjitāḥ
puro niṣpratibhā dīpāstasyāsaṃllajjitā iva
praṇatāndṛktribhāgena bhūmipālānvilokayan
nāmabhir vikramodāraiḥ sūcitānvetrimaṇḍalaiḥ
sa babhau gatilolena hāreṇa tuhinatviṣā
sudhākallolajālena pādadāreṇa manmathaḥ
śrīmānsamprāpya śibiraṃ śubhraṃ śantanujanmanaḥ
śayānaṃ ratnaparyaṅke praṇanāma vilokya tam
rājñeti pūjitastena kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ
duryodhanaḥ kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā pitāmahamabhāṣata
ayaṃ jetā bhṛgubhuvaḥ kārmukapraṇayī tava
bhujastrailokyavijaye paryāpta iti me matiḥ
kāruṇyādānṛśaṃsyādvā rakṣyāste yadi pāṇḍavāḥ
tatkarṇamanujānīhi yuddhāya raṇakarkaśam
ityuktaḥ kururājena marmaṇīva samāhataḥ
prabhāte drakṣyasītyuktvā niḥśvasankṣmāmalokayat
kauravo 'pi tamāmantrya nijaṃ śibiramāyayau
diśaḥ śabalayankṣiptaṃ dīpadīptair vibhūṣaṇaiḥ
atha prabhāte bhīṣmeṇa droṇadrauṇimukhaiḥ saha
vihite sarvatobhadre vyūhe vyūhāgravartinā
prativyūheṣvanīkeṣu nadadbhiḥ pāṇḍunandanaiḥ
abhimanyuḥ kurucamūragre vīro vyadārayat
śarāṃśuśataduṣprekṣyaṃ nidāghārkamivodyatam
na sehire taṃ bhūpālā māninaḥ saṃhatā api
duryodhanaprerito 'tha rakṣaḥpatiralambusaḥ
tamabhyadhāvadbibhrāṇo māyāṃ trailokyamohinīm
tasya nādena mahatā jagatpralayaśaṃsinā
nipetuḥ sahasā yodhā bahavo vigatāsavaḥ
draupadeyaiḥ puraḥ prāptaiḥ sa vidhāya raṇaṃ kṣaṇam
abhimanyuratha bāṇaiḥ samaṃ dehamivākarot
śaranirdāritenātha vihitāṃ tena rakṣasā
saubhadrastāmasīṃ māyāṃ cichedārkāstratejasā
atha drauṇiprabhṛtibhiḥ sātyakipramukhā yudhi
saṃsaktā gaganaṃ cakrurdivyāstradahanākulam
arjuno droṇamabhyetya mahāstragrāmaduḥsaham
vāyavyāstreṇa vidadhe jagatāṃ kṣobhavibhramam
samudīrya ca śailāstraṃ drauṇena kṣapite 'nale
dhanaṃjayaḥ kurucamūṃ śarajālairapūrayat
bhīmabhīmagadāghātanirbhinne gajamaṇḍale
susrāva śoṇitanadī patākāphenamālinī
tasmin ākulasaṃgrāme vartamāne bhayaṃkare
vetāladattatāleṣu nṛtyatsu chinnamūrdhasu
bhīṣmaḥ pṛthuśarajvālāduḥsahaḥ subhaṭendhanaḥ
jajvāla cāpakreṅkāramantrapūta ivānalaḥ
tadbhujapreritāḥ kṣipraṃ sāyakā viviśurnṛpān
vihaṅgā iva sāyāhne ghanacchāyānmahīruhān
khadyotā iva vṛkṣeṣu śalabhā iva śāliṣu
bhīṣmabāṇā narendreṣu peturhaṃsāḥ sahaḥsviva
nikṛttaiścāmaroṣṇīṣaiśchannāśca pṛthivībhujām
cakāra samare bhīṣmaḥ svayaśoviṣadā diśaḥ
rājñāṃ śirobhiḥ pṛthivīmāstīrya pulakojjvalaḥ
raṇalakṣmyāḥ sa vidadhe kelipadmākarāniva
śirastraśaranirgharṣajātā vahnikaṇā babhuḥ
rājñāṃ hatānāṃ bhīṣmeṇa jīvā iva nabhaścarāḥ
ghanena śarajālena grastā lokena sarvataḥ
sa cakre sarvasainyānām akāṇḍarajanībhramam
vidīrṇe pāṇḍavabale chinnavarmarathadhvaje
gajānīkeṣu bhagneṣu bhāgaśeṣeṣu rājasu
lajjāmutsṛjya yāteṣu tyaktacāpeṣu keśavaḥ
satyasaṃdhaṃ raṇe bhīṣmaṃ jahītyarjunamabravīt
dhanaṃjayo 'tha niḥśvasya viṣaṇṇavadanāmbujaḥ
nindanmuhuḥ kṣattradharmaṃ pitāmahamupādravat
dṛṣṭvā gāṇḍīvadhanvānamudyataṃ śaravarṣiṇam
bale tūrṇamupāvṛtte punaryuyudhire bhaṭāḥ
bhīṣmacāpacyutairbāṇaiśchāditaṃ vīkṣya phalguṇam
rathamutsṛjya kaṃsāristamadhāvadbhujāyudhaḥ
vilokya kupitaṃ bhīṣmaḥ svayaṃ kṛṣṇamabhidrutam
uvāca dhanyatāmānī pulakālaṃkṛtākṛtiḥ
puṇyabhājāmahaṃ dhuryo bhagavankṛtināṃ varaḥ
yasya tvaṃ jagatāṃ nātho vadhāya svayamudyataḥ
iti vādini gāṅgeye rathāttūrṇaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
avaruhya tataḥ kṛṣṇamānināya rathaṃ punaḥ
athārjunaśarāsārairākīrṇe kurukānane
punaḥ śāntanavaścakre saṃhāraṃ pṛthivībhujām
ghore vyatikare tasminbhagne subhaṭamaṇḍale
avahāramakurvanta dinānte pāṇḍunandanāḥ
tato rajanyāṃ vijane dharmarājo janārdanam
jagāda rājakaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhinnaṃ bhīṣmeṇa duḥkhitaḥ
paśya kṛṣṇa prabuddhena gāṅgeyavaḍavāgninā
sainyāmbudhiraparyante mama nīto 'lpaśeṣatām
maṇḍalīkṛtacāpasya sahasrāṃśuśatatviṣaḥ
bhīṣmasyākhaṇḍalo 'pyagre satyaṃ paribhāvāspadam
alaṃ rājyena me tāvaditi vādini dharmaje
uvāca śauriryotsye 'haṃ svayaṃ śantanunandanam
nākārya me bhavatkāryamutsṛṣṭasamayo 'dhunā
pālayāmi raṇe bhīṣmaṃ paśyatāṃ jagatībhujām
etadākarṇya kṛṣṇoktaṃ babhāṣe pāṇḍavāgrajaḥ
na mithyāvādinaṃ kāmāttvāṃ kuryāmahamacyuta
jayopāyamito gatvā bhīṣmaṃ pṛcchāmi bhūtale
sa hi māmāśiṣā pūrvaṃ vātsalyātsamayojayat
iti niścitya kṛṣṇena bhrātṛbhiśca sahāśu kṛt
jagāma bhīṣmaśibiraṃ gūḍhacārī yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
sa praṇamyānujasakhaḥ śauryarāśiṃ pitāmaham
papraccha vijayopāyaṃ sa ca pṛṣṭastamabravīt
na taṃ paśyāmi lokeṣu vīro māṃ vijayeta yaḥ
jayalābhe ca yuṣmākaṃ mayi jīvati kā kathā
na viśastrena saṃtraste na strīpūrve mameṣavaḥ
patanti tasmātklībena māṃ ghātaya śikhaṇḍinā
ukte devavrateneti lajjāvinamitānanaḥ
akāma iva duḥkhena yayau svaśibiraṃ nṛpaḥ
tataḥ prabhāte vyūheṣu sainyeṣu subhaṭairmithaḥ
śikhaṇḍipramukhā vīrāḥ parānīkamupādravan
tato bhīṣmaśaraśreṇīlulite rājamaṇḍale
śikhaṇḍī dhutakodaṇḍaścaṇḍakopastamabhyadhāt
tamabravīcchāntanavaḥ kāmaṃ prahara pārṣata
nanāma bhīṣmaviśikhāḥ patantyanujane jane
iti vādinamabhyetya maṇḍalīkṛtakārmukaḥ
śikhaṇḍī niḥśvasankopādāpageyamabhāṣata
jetāraṃ bhārgavasyāpi jānāmi tvāṃ mahaujasam
yudhi yudhyasva vā mā vā na me jīvangamiṣyasi
uktvaitadbāṇajālena pārṣataḥ samapūrayat
rakṣyamāṇaḥ samabhyetya paścādgāṇḍīvadhanvanā
bhīṣmo 'pi tam anādṛtya viddhvā kṛṣṇārjunau śaraiḥ
viveśa pāṇḍavacamūṃ rājaveṇuvanānalaḥ
dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhairvīraiḥ kauravāṇāṃ tarasvinām
dāruṇo 'tha prahāro 'bhūd rajaḥpihitadiṅmukhaḥ
tato droṇiprabhṛtayo vīrā droṇasya śāsanāt
rakṣantaḥ samare bhīṣmaṃ dhanaṃjayamayodhayan
tataḥ śāntanavo rājñāṃ śarairaśanigauravaiḥ
mauliratnāṃśuśabalaṃ samunmathya virocanam
ākrīḍamiva kālasya vidhāya kadanaṃ raṇe
abravītkūṇitamanā dūrādeva yudhiṣṭhiram
vadhāya kuru kaunteya yatnaṃ me nṛpatikṣayāt
viṣaṇṇo 'haṃ bhṛśaṃ putra raudreṇānena karmaṇā
iti vādini gāṅgeye śithilīkṛtakārmuke
sṛñjayāḥ saha pāñcālaiḥ somakaiśca sahādravan
tataḥ kurucamūvīrāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathān
āvārya bhīṣmarakṣāyai dvandvaṃ yuddhāni cakrire
atha gāṅgeyaviśikhairaprayatnojjhitairapi
avartata mahāraudro rājajīvitasaṃkṣayaḥ
tamabhyadhāvad ākarṇākṛṣṭakodaṇḍamaṇḍalaḥ
śikhaṇḍī khaṇḍaparaśuprabhāvaṃ phalguṇeritaḥ
svayaṃ duryodhanenātha preritāṃ vīkṣya vāhinīm
tasminsvabhaṭasaṃhāre vartamāne pitāmahaḥ
udīrya ghoraṃ divyāstramabhyadhāvaddhanaṃjayam
athārjunasyāgrametya śikhaṇḍini puraḥsthite
vimānā iva gāṅgeyo mahāstraṃ saṃjahāra tat
brahmalokābhikāmeṣu yudhyamāneṣu rājasu
vīrāṇāṃ bhīṣmaviśikhairayuteṣu patatsu ca
dārayantaṃ parānīkaṃ tametya vasavo 'bruvan
bhīṣma saṃnyāsakālo 'yaṃ tavāsmadabhikāṅkṣitaḥ
tataḥ ślathodyame tasminprasanne bhuvanatraye
arjunapramukhāḥ sarve sāyakaistamapūrayan
chidyamāneṣu bāleṣu tasya tūrṇaṃ kirīṭinā
śikhaṇḍī prāhiṇottasmai hemapuṅkhaśarāvalīm
śaikhaṇḍīṃ śaramālāṃ tāṃ śairīṣīm iva peśalām
jagrāha prahasanbhīṣmaḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthagitakārmukaḥ
duryodhanasamādiṣṭānbhīṣmasya ratharakṣiṇaḥ
mohayanbāṇajālena phalguṇastamavākirat
vidāryamāṇo nīrandhrairgāṇḍīvānniḥsṛtaiḥ śaraiḥ
duḥśāsanaṃ pārśvagataṃ bhīṣmaḥ sasmitamabravīt
naite śikhaṇḍino bāṇāḥ śilāsaṃghātabhedinaḥ
viśanti mama marmāṇi bilaṃ viṣadharā iva
ete te vajrasaṃsparśā nivātakavacacchidaḥ
śarīrahāriṇo ghorāḥ kirātaraṇasākṣiṇaḥ
ityuktvā pāṇḍuputrāya śaktiṃ cikṣepa śaktimān
tāṃ ca śakrasutastūrṇaṃ cakāra viśikhaistridhā
sarvāyudheṣu chinneṣu tato gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
kṣaṇādbabhūva durlakṣyo bhīṣmo nirvivaraiḥ śaraiḥ
yudhyamāneṣu vīreṣu bhūtāviṣṭeṣvivākulam
dāruṇe tumule tasminnirvibhāge baladvaye
aparāhṇe rathādbhīṣmaḥ sahasrāṃśurivāparaḥ
aspṛṣṭabhūmir viśikhaiḥ papāta mahasāṃ nidhiḥ
tasminnipatite vīre ketau sarvadhanuṣmatām
mahatāmapi vīrāṇāṃ hṛdayāni cakampire
tato nivṛtte saṃgrāme hāhākāre nabhaḥspṛśi
divyaṃ bheje nijaṃ bhāvamaluptātmā pitāmahaḥ
ākampamāne bhuvane vāguvācāśarīriṇī
bhīṣma kālaṃ pratīkṣasva yogavānuttarāyaṇam
sarvajña dhāraya prāṇānsvacchandanidhano hṛdi
śrutvaitatparamaṃ yogamāsasāda suravrataḥ
tatastridaśavāhinyā visṛṣṭā haṃsarūpiṇaḥ
tamevārthaṃ samabhyetya munayo bhīṣmamabruvan
sthito 'smīti ca gāṅgeyo nigadya yaśasāṃ nidhiḥ
śaratalpe gataḥ sarvānkurūnbhītānasāntvayat
praṇatānatha samprāptānpunaḥ kauravapāṇḍavān
aśrupūrṇekṣaṇānūce saṃbhāvya kurupuṃgavaḥ
dhāraṇaṃ lambamānasya śiraso me vidhīyatām
śrutvaitadupadhāneṣu samānīteṣu rājabhiḥ
jagrāha śāsanāttasya tribhiḥ pārthaḥ śaraiḥ śiraḥ
bhīṣmastatkarmatuṣṭo 'tha praśaśaṃsa dhanaṃjayam
pāṇḍavaiḥ kriyatāṃ saṃdhirityuvāca ca kauravam
tato rajanyāṃ yātāyāmupāviṣṭeṣu rājasu
sevyamāno munijanairbhīṣmo jalamayācata
maṇikāñcanacitreṣu kalaśeṣvamalāmbhasaḥ
samānīteṣu bhūpālairvyadhānmeghāstramarjunaḥ
tadudbhūtena payasā gāṅgeyastena tarpitaḥ
narāvatāraṃ prītātmā sādaraṃ tamapūjayat
mahāratheṣu yāteṣu samāmantryāpagāsutam
karṇaḥ prasādayāmāsa tadabhyarcya kṛtāñjaliḥ
tamuvāca prasannātmā vītamanyuḥ pitāmahaḥ
bhajasva pārtheṣu śamaṃ vīrāste bhrātarastava
vaikartanastadākarṇya jagāda vinatānanaḥ
jāne sarvamavaśyaṃ tu bhavitavyamidaṃ prabho
kiṃtu duryodhanasyārthe suhṛdo mānakāriṇaḥ
anujānīhi māṃ tāta samarāya samudyatam
iti bruvāṇo bhīṣmeṇa so 'nujñāto varūthinīm
prayayau kuruputrāṇāṃ rathena ghananādinā
atha kuruvṛṣabhāṇām aṅgarājotsukānāṃ paraparibhavadīkṣābhagnamānādarāṇām
patihitamanīkaṃ sāmyamāpa drutānāṃ sarayapavanapālīkampitānāṃ vanānām
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam
devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet
suravrataṃ hataṃ śrutvā dhṛtarāṣṭro 'tiduḥkhitaḥ
muhurmuhuryaśorāśiṃ tamaśocadariṃdamam
punaḥ saṃgrāmamālokya samāyāto 'tha saṃjayaḥ
pṛṣṭo vaicitravīryeṇa vīrasaṃhāramabhyadhāt
tato bhīṣme hate rājankuravo bhṛśaduḥkhitāḥ
abdhau bhagne pravahaṇe vaṇijaḥ patitā iva
vāñchitaṃ samare śarma dadṛśuḥ karṇamāgatam
vikrītāḥ paradeśeṣu snigdhaṃ bandhumivāpadi
tato duryodhanaḥ śokaṃ saṃstambhya dhṛtisāgaraḥ
karṇasyānumate cakre droṇaṃ senāsu nāyakam
tenābhiṣikto vidhivadguruḥ sarvadhanuṣmatām
sa babhau śaktimānvīro mahāsena ivāparaḥ
vṛddhasya svayaśaḥśubhraṃ chattraṃ tasya vyarocata
dugdhodadheriva śrīmaccandramaṇḍalamudyatam
āmuktahemakavacaḥ sa dīptaḥ kiraṇairbabhau
upasthitaiḥ kṛtyakāle divyāstrairiva sevitaḥ
praṇetā sarvavīrāṇāṃ sadṛśaḥ prājyatejasā
sākṣādiva dhanurvedaḥ saṃhārasyāgamāvadhiḥ
reje rathena raukmena śoṇāśvena patākinā
saṃdhyājuṣā nirjhariṇā meruṇeva divākaraḥ
virarāja rathe tasya śātakaumbhaḥ kamaṇḍaluḥ
śauryoṣmaṇā pratigataḥ pratāpa iva piṇḍitaḥ
ākarṇapalitaḥ śyāmo dhaureyaḥ sarvadhanvinām
dadau varaṃ śriyā juṣṭaḥ sa rājñā svayamarthitaḥ
jīvagrāhaṃ samādāya rājānaṃ te yudhiṣṭhiram
hate 'rjune pradāsyāmi paśyatāṃ sarvabhūbhujām
etadguruvaco rājā pratigṛhya kṛtāñjaliḥ
viśrāvya nijasenāsu tūryanādotsavaṃ vyadhāt
tacca dharmasuto jñātvā saha gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
krauñcavyūhaṃ samādhāya saṃnaddho yoddhumudyayau
droṇena śakaṭavyūhe nirmite bhṛśasaṃhate
avartata mahadyuddhaṃ vīrāṇāṃ dehaśātanam
tataḥ sṛñjayapāñcālamatsyasenāsu duḥsahāḥ
śarīrahāriṇaḥ petur droṇanāmāṅkitāḥ śarāḥ
bhidyamāneṣu sainyeṣu nipatadgajavājiṣu
raktakallolinīvegairnīteṣu syandaneṣvapi
yudhiṣṭhiramukhānvīrānkopāddroṇamabhidrutān
avārayansusaṃrabdhāndroṇikarṇakṛpādayaḥ
abhimanyurathākṛṣya rathātkeśeṣu pauravam
apātayatkṛpāṇena paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
tatkopāt khaḍgamādāya jayadrathamupāgatam
śalyaṃ ca virathaṃ vīro vidadhe balināṃ varam
tataḥ śalyo gadāpāṇiḥ padbhyāṃ saubhadramādravat
gadayā vīravārinyā bhīmaśca tamavārayat
tayoḥ parasparāghātakīrṇavahnikaṇākulam
nṛṇāṃ vimohanaṃ ghoraṃ gadāyuddhamavartata
maṇḍalāni carantau tau samadāviva kuñjarau
abhipatya padānyaṣṭau gadābhyāṃ jaghnaturmithaḥ
gāḍhaprahārasaṃjātamūrchāvihvalamānasau
tau dṛṣṭvā patitau vīrāḥ saṃnipetuḥ prahāriṇaḥ
nīte madrādhipe tūrṇaṃ rathena kṛtavarmaṇā
bhīmasenaḥ samādāya kurusenāmadārayat
karṇasūnoratha śarair dṛṣasenasya pāṇḍavāḥ
ākīrṇāndraupadīputrānvilokya tamupādravan
tato rukmaratho droṇaḥ svayaṃ pāñcālavāhinīm
praviśya bāṇairvidadhe viprakīrṇāṃ sahasradhā
śikhaṇḍisātyakimukhānsa vidārya mahārathān
yudhiṣṭhiram abhiprekṣuḥ kurvannarapatikṣayam
yugaṃdharaṃ vyāghradattaṃ siṃhasenaṃ ca pārthivam
nināya mṛtyusadanaṃ śarairaśanidāruṇaiḥ
tiṣṭha sthito 'haṃ yudhyasva hato 'sīti muhurmuhuḥ
droṇāgre yudhyamānānāṃ bhūbhujāmabhavadraṇaḥ
droṇena yudhyamānānāṃ niśamya śvetavāhanaḥ
kolāhalaṃ svasainyānāṃ tūrṇaṃ taṃ deśamāyayau
sa nihatyāstrajālena vīraḥ kuruvarūthinīm
vidadhe raktataṭinīmāvartahṛtakuñjarām
tato 'vahāraṃ sainyānāṃ pārthasāyakapīḍitāḥ
yāte 'staṃ tigmakiraṇe cakrire kurupuṃgavāḥ
niśāyāṃ saṃniviṣṭeṣu śibire sarvarājasu
lajjamāna ivācāryo duryodhanamabhāṣata
uktameva mayā rājanrahitaṃ savyasācinā
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ grahīṣyāmi durjayo hi dhanaṃjayaḥ
iti bruvāṇe vailakṣyādācārye rājasaṃnidhau
trigarvarājaḥ provāca kṛtavairaḥ kirīṭinā
vayaṃ saṃśaptakagaṇairmālavaistuṇḍilaistathā
vīrairmadrakakāmbojalalitaiśca prahāribhiḥ
rathāyutaistribhiḥ pārthamāhūya pṛthagāsthitaḥ
yotsyāmahe suprakṛtairiti satyaṃ śapāmahe
ityukte śapathaṃ kṛtvā trigartā vahnisākṣiṇaḥ
pratyūṣe niryayurvīrāḥ suśarmapramukhā nṛpāḥ
te turaṅgakharoddhūtadhūligrastanabhastalāḥ
cakrire phalguṇāhvānaṃ nādaiḥ pralayaśaṃsibhiḥ
tānvyūhenārdhacandreṇa same deśe vyavasthitān
dṛṣṭvā pārthastadāhūto yudhiṣṭhiramabhāṣata
anujānātu māmāryastrigartānāṃ vadhaṃ prati
ete māmabhivāñchanti yoddhuṃ saṃgharṣaśālinaḥ
ayaṃ te satyajidvīraḥ pāñcālyaḥ pravaro rathaḥ
goptā droṇābhisaraṇe śakratulyaparākramaḥ
ityuktvā caṇḍagāṇḍīvaghoṣaghaṇṭitadiktaṭaḥ
pralayāmbhodasaṃrabdhastānyayau kapiketanaḥ
te 'pi pāṇḍavamāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā pramadanirbharāḥ
phullasālamivādṛśyaṃ cakruḥ kṣipraṃ śilīmukhaiḥ
tataḥ śauryāmbudheḥ phenamaṭṭahāsaṃ raṇaśriyaḥ
dadhmau dhanaṃjayaḥ śaṅkhaṃ kandaṃ nijayaśastaroḥ
tasya śabdena mahatā tatsainyaṃ bhayakāriṇā
abhūnnivṛttamātaṅgaṃ stimitāṅgaturaṅgamam
atha sāyakajālena jīvamatsyāpahāriṇā
trigartavāhinīṃ pārthaḥ samantātparyavārayat
tataḥ saṃśaptakagaṇotsṛṣṭair avivaraiḥ śaraiḥ
pihite bhuvanābhoge babhūvākālaśarvarī
tataḥ pravidadhe tvāṣṭraṃ mahāstraṃ vajrinandanaḥ
yenārjunasahasrāṇi dadṛśuste sasaṃbhramāḥ
jahārākarṇakṛṣṭena bhallena ca mahaujasaḥ
sphuranmauliprabhājālaṃ śiraḥ kāyātsudhanvanaḥ
tatpreṣitāṃ śastravṛṣṭiṃ pavanāstreṇa hāriṇā
vidhūya tacchiraḥpuñjairadṛśyāṃ vidadhe mahīm
chinnacchattradhvajarathaṃ patadbhujabhaṭānanam
trigartakadanaṃ pārtho ghoramāyodhanaṃ vyadhāt
asminkṣaṇe vainateyavyūhe droṇena nirmite
vyūhena nirmitārdhena pāṇḍuputrāḥ samudyayuḥ
tataḥ pravṛtte saṃgrāme kṣaye caiva mahībhujām
dhṛṣṭadyumnaprabhṛtayo droṇamukhyānayodhayan
rajobhiḥ pihite vyomni dikṣu ruddhāsu sāyakaiḥ
avibhāgamamaryādaṃ ghoraṃ yuddhamavartata
abhidrute tato droṇe dharmarājajighṛkṣayā
ghoro halahalāśabdaḥ sainyānāmudabhūtkṣaṇam
kālāgnitejasaṃ vīraṃ dhaureyaṃ sarvadhanvinām
avārayitum abhyetya satyajitsatyavikramaḥ
yudhyamānaṃ tato hatvā vṛkaṃ rājasutaṃ guruḥ
śaraiḥ satyajitaṃ cakre kīrṇāṃśumiva bhāskaram
hemanāmāṅkitairbāṇairmuhūrtādatha satyajit
dīptairapūrayaddroṇaṃ khadyotairiva pādapam
tataḥ satyajitaḥ kāyādācāryaḥ śauryaśālinaḥ
śiro jahāra bhallena caṇḍatāṇḍavakuṇḍalam
nipātite satyajiti pravare sarvadhanvinām
vidrute dharmatanaye vyadīryata varūthinī
hṛtvānujaṃ virāṭasya śatānīkaṃ prahāriṇam
dṛḍhasenaṃ kṣatradevaṃ vasudānaṃ ca pārthivam
nighnanrukmarathaścedimatsyapāñcālasṛñjayān
vidadhe rudhirāvartaiḥ kṛtāntodyānavāhinīm
vidrute pāṇḍavabale pīḍite droṇasāyakaiḥ
karṇaduryodhanamukhā bhāradvājamapūjayan
punarāvartite sainye bhīmena bhujaśālinā
saṃhatāḥ pṛthivīpālāḥ kopāddroṇamupādravan
ṛṣyavarṇairhayairbhīmaḥ sātyakiḥ sphāṭikaprabhaiḥ
pārāvataprabhaiścāśvairdhṛṣṭadyumnaścamūpatiḥ
nakulaḥ sahadevaśca śukatittirisaprabhaiḥ
abhimanyuḥ piśaṅgābhaiḥ pāṇḍyaiśca tuhinaprabhaiḥ
dantaprabhaiḥ kṛṣṇavālaiḥ svayaṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
anye tu vividhacchāyaiścitravarmāmbaradhvajaiḥ
parivārya raṇe droṇaṃ cakrurbāṇamayaṃ jagat
mṛdaṅganādakau rājño dhvajo nandopanandakau
divyayantreṇa vihitau babhaturdharmajanmanaḥ
dharmānilendrāśvināṃ ca pratimā draupadībhuvām
tumule yudhyamānānāṃ rejire kāñcanojjvalāḥ
āvṛtaṃ droṇamālokya rājabhiḥ krūrayā dhiyā
duryodhanādayo vīrānbhīmamukhyānsamāpatan
teṣu śalyapradhāneṣu yudhiṣṭhirapurogamaiḥ
dvandvayuddhaniṣakteṣu samarotsavarājiṣu
kṛtabāhau subāhau ca hate vīre yuyutsunā
vaṅgarāje samātaṅge bhīmasenena pātite
vidrute kauravabale nihateṣvabhimāniṣu
nirālokeṣu lokeṣu rajastimiramaṇḍalaiḥ
prerito bhagadattena saṃvartakaghanaprabhaḥ
supratīko madoddāmaḥ pāṇḍusenāṃ vyagāhata
daityasaṃgrāmasāhāyye jambhāribhavanasthitaḥ
airāvaṇaghaṭābandhaḥ pramāṇaṃ yasya varṣmaṇaḥ
śaśiśubhrairnakhair udyād ekapāt sa kṣaṇaṃ babhau
svamahīpīḍanaruṣā daṣṭaḥ śeṣaśatairiva
itaścandrārkamukhyānāṃ prabhavaḥ sarvatejasām
iti nakṣatramālābhir udayādririvāśritaḥ
digvāraṇaraṇāvāptiṃ vinā vyarthamidaṃ balam
itīva pṛthuśūtkārairniḥśaśvāsa madālasaḥ
etā āyāntu vaiklavyaṃ matpratāpoṣmaṇā diśaḥ
itīva karṇatālābhyāṃ muhurmuhuravījayat
caṇḍīśaḍamaroccaṇḍaḍiṇḍimadhvānaniḥsvanaiḥ
helayonmīlayankiṃcillocane pracacāla saḥ
bhagadattāstraniṣkṛttavīravaktrāñcitāṃ mahīm
gatvā pade pade paśyansasmāra kamalākarān
sa vāhinīṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ praviśya nibiḍaṃ gajaḥ
gajavājirathān piṃṣan vasākardaminīṃ vyadhāt
mṛdyamānāḥ karīndreṇa tāḥ senāḥ kauravadviṣām
saṃkocamāpuḥ sahasā darpeṇeva vibhūtayaḥ
tena mandaratulyena gajenānīkavāridheḥ
samākrāntasya nistriṃśakālakūṭacchaṭā babhuḥ
kuṇḍalīkṛtaśuṇḍāgraḥ so 'bhyadhāvadvṛkodaram
ākṛṣṭaṃ pāśahastena yena taṃ menire janāḥ
saṃśaye patitaṃ bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā tūrṇaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
saha sarvairmahīpālairbhagadattaṃ samabhyadhāt
sa taiḥ parivṛto vīrairhatvā dāśārṇabhūpatim
unmamātha rathaṃ vegātsupratīkena sātyakeḥ
tasya śīkariṇā ghoraśītkṛtenātha dantinaḥ
bhīmasenamukhā dūraṃ jahrustrastāsturaṅgamān
sā senā bhagadattena kuñjarasthena pīḍitā
janatā kunṛpeṇeva na lebhe śaraṇaṃ kvacit
gajānāṃ patyamānānāṃ rathānāṃ sphuṭatāmapi
hāhākāraiśca bhītānāṃ niḥsvanastumulo 'bhavat
sveṣāmākrandamākarṇya vajrāstreṇendranandanaḥ
trigartānsānugānhatvā bhagadattamathāpatat
dṛṣṭvā gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ tārkṣyavat tūrṇamāgatam
prerito bhagadattena kruddho 'dhāvaddvipādhipaḥ
tamantakamivāyāntamapasavyena keśavaḥ
rathena moghasaṃrambhaṃ kṛtvā punarabhūtpuraḥ
viddhvā śarasahasreṇa pārthaṃ prāgjyotiṣeśvaraḥ
nārāyaṇāstramasṛjattacca jagrāha keśavaḥ
arjunaṃ rakṣatastūrṇaṃ tadastraṃ kaiṭabhadviṣaḥ
niṣaktaṃ vakṣasi prāpa hemasragdāmavibhramam
tasminviphalatāṃ yāte mahāstre dīptatejasi
vailakṣyādarjunaḥ kṛṣṇamuvācāsphālayandhanuḥ
nūnaṃ yuddheṣvayogyo 'haṃ yenāstraṃ dhṛtavānasi
śrutvaitadavadatpārthaṃ mānayangaruḍadhvajaḥ
caturmūrtibhṛtā pūrvaṃ pṛthivīvacasā mayā
vitīrṇaṃ narakāyaitannijāstraṃ bhūmisūnave
amoghamāptavāṃstasmād daityātso 'sau narādhipaḥ
gṛhītaṃ tanmayā divyaṃ jahyenamadhunā nṛpam
ukte janārdaneneti savyasācī sakuñjaram
ūrdhvavaktraiḥ śaraiḥ kṣipraṃ bhagadattamapūrayat
girivarṣmagajārūḍho bāṇaiḥ prāgjyotiṣeśvaraḥ
adūravidrutāmartyavimānam akaronnabhaḥ
tataḥ karṇāntakṛṣṭena kumbhayoḥ kuñjareśvaram
āpucchagāminā pārtho nārācenākulaṃ vyadhāt
sa phalguṇeṣunirbhinnaḥ patan dviradabhūdharaḥ
jaghāna mahatīṃ senāṃ patitāḥ pātayanti yat
kruddhastato 'rdhacandreṇa hṛdi viddhaḥ kirīṭinā
muktāṅkuśadhanurbāṇo bhagadatto 'bhavadvyasuḥ
tasminnipatite vīre kakude sarvabhūbhujām
vijaye kurusenānāmāśābandhaḥ ślatho 'bhavat
vidrute kauravānīke saubalau vṛṣakācalau
gāndhārau dhanvināṃ dhuryau dhanaṃjayamayudhyatām
tau bāṇavarṣiṇau pārthaśareṇaikena saṃhatau
syūtāvapātayatprītyā yāto bhāruṇḍatāmiva
anujau nihatau dṛṣṭvā śakuniḥ kopakampitaḥ
kalpayanvipulāṃ māyāṃ savyasācināmādravat
astraiśca krūrasatvaiśca tamobhiścābhito vṛtaḥ
nākampata raṇe pārthastasya māyāśatairapi
saureṇāstreṇa tanmāyāṃ chittvā kātaramohinīm
prāhiṇotsāyakānyena śakuniḥ prayayau bhayāt
yāte 'rjunamayaṃ lokaṃ manyamāne 'tha saubale
na lebhe śaraṇaṃ trāsādvidrutā kuruvāhinī
tato droṇaḥ sahānīkairyudhiṣṭhirajighṛkṣayā
haranvaktrāṇi vīrāṇāṃ pāñcālānsamupādravat
vadhyamāneṣvanīkeṣu śoṇāśvena sahasraśaḥ
raktāsavamadeneva cakampe vasudhāvadhūḥ
tūrṇaṃ praharata droṇaṃ tūrṇaṃ rakṣata saṃgare
